About the job
Status: Full-time
Reporting to: Supervisor, Master Data Services
 Job Scope:
Reporting to the Supervisor of Mater Data Services (MDS), the primary responsibility of this role is to support the company’s master data accuracy, ensuring overall data integrity is maintained in Gay Lea’s business applications, including the ERP and Warehouse Management Systems by analyzing business request for compliance and accuracy prior to data entry. This position specializes in identifying, investigating, and resolving master data discrepancies and providing master data support to all Gay Lea departments as required (e.g. audits, balancing accounts, reporting). 
 Key Responsibilities: 
Review, analyze and consult with the business to ensure data/field accuracy for the intended data location
Input, monitor and maintain consistency and integrity of master data
Identify, analyze and resolve data issues and/or system errors
Apply data audit and validation methods and procedures to ensure data quality
Utilized internal Master Data field library to collaborate with the data owners on ensure data and field compliance. Escalate to data governance council when required
Understand end-to-end business processes to provide data management and integrity expertise
Meet service level agreements as agreed upon with the business
Complete daily, weekly and monthly data integrity tasks
Provide daily support of the ERP and Warehouse Management Systems; manage and resolve support tickets
Contribute to the continuous improvement of the department
 Qualifications: 
Post-Secondary education in Business or Computer Programming
Excellent attention to detail with a high level of accuracy
Strong analytical and problem-solving skills
Proficient with computers (Microsoft Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Access, Outlook)
Advanced knowledge of Microsoft Excel for data manipulation
SQL experience is considered an asset
Solid organizational and multi-tasking skills with the ability to work in a fast-paced environment
Effective communication and interpersonal skills (written and verbal)
Previous experience with D365 /other ERP or Warehouse Management System is an asset

Gay Lea Foods is a proud Canadian-owned dairy food and beverage company with a robust portfolio that includes 7 established brands such as Gay Lea Butter, Nordica Cottage Cheese, Ivanhoe Cheese, Salerno Cheese, and Hewitt’s Dairy. Our wide range of products are sold in Retail, Foodservice, Industrial, Co-pack, and Export markets, developed and produced out of our 13 manufacturing facilities in Ontario and Alberta.
Delivering high-quality and innovative products - from the consumer favourite Spreadables and North America’s first Smooth™ Cottage Cheese, to Nothing But Cheese™, an innovative snack made with 100% cheese, is what makes us market leaders in our categories. Our grassroots approach to business is what guides our direction and differentiates us from our competitors.
 Our employees inspire our culture of excellence and entrepreneurship. We hire innovative and passionate professionals who know that greatness is achieved through people, partnerships, and acting with a business owner mindset. 
For more about us visit: http://www.gaylea.com

Join us!   Job Summary 

The Expert, Data Analysis is responsible for conducting detailed analysis and providing access to advanced analytics solutions to solve business problems, while leveraging statistical and optimization techniques. The role handles and governs large quantities of data from multiple data sources, including the ability to merge it and ensure its consistency. Moreover, the role encompasses the development and creation of visualization and analysis tools to be used by internal stakeholders. It involves seeking out and understanding new data sources, merging it with other sources, and modelling in order to provide a consumable format for analysis and presentation at an executive level. The incumbent contributes to enabling automation and supports better and faster data-driven decisions making in virtually every aspect of its business.

 Main Responsibilities   Data Management & Analytics 

Find and interpret rich data sources, merge and ensure consistency of datasets
Handle large amounts of data despite hardware, software, and bandwidth constraints
Query large datasets and link related factors to reveal performance, safety or cost-saving opportunities
Analyze data, spot trends, and bring change to the organization
Develop initiatives to assist Financial Planning team in leveraging data to draw causal relationships between financial information and operating KPIs in the respective functions (Transportation, Engineering, Mechanical, etc.)
Assist in understanding sensitivities, impacts of change, and draw insights on action items that can positively impact operations while being cognizant of ripple effects on other areas of the business.
Use data science techniques to find data patterns, anomalies, and optimization opportunities
Interpret, translate, and communicate analytical findings to business stakeholders
Tackle and solve complex analytical problems using quantitative approaches

 Data reporting and visualisation 

Create visualizations to aid in understanding data and build mathematical models
Provide analytical support by creating and sharing regular and ad hoc reports as required in a format that can be easily consumed and interpreted by internal customers
Develop and optimize Tableau and Power BI reports and applications to deliver simplified analytics to support insight development

Center of Expertise

Stay abreast of market best practices
Autonomously identify the best approach, process, and tools for the function
Educate internal stakeholders on data visualization

 Working Conditions 

The role has standard working conditions in an office environment with a regular workweek from Monday to Friday. The role is eligible to participate in CN’s flexible work policy. Due to the nature of the role, the incumbent must be able to meet tight deadlines, handle pressure, and stress.

Requirements Experience

Relational Databases and Modeling

About the job
Joining Suncor means you will work for one of the best companies in Canada, providing tremendous future potential where talented people thrive and lead. As our business evolves, so do our employment opportunities. Our work culture includes a dynamic mix of professionals, with a diversity of skills and expertise.

We are looking for a Quantitative Analyst to join our Risk Management team! This role offers the opportunity to optimize and be creative in automating processes.

You will be responsible to provide quantitative analysis within our risk management department, creating extensive models, computational analyses, and visualization to value structured deals and assess market risk associated with Suncor’s trading operations.

Minimum Requirements: 

Experience with finance principles (P/L, price curves, hedging, financial instruments)
Experience in the energy market space, including a deep understanding of crude, refined products, natural gas, and power markets as well as spreads, basis, and diffs (time, location, quality)
Strong background in development of risk analytics, risk metrics, and valuation of non-linear instruments
Proficiency in Power BI, and Power Apps, and strong programming skills in SQL, VBA, Matlab, and Python
University degree in applied mathematics, engineering, mathematical finance, or physics OR equivalent
Deep knowledge of linear algebra, statistics, time series analysis, and econometrics
University degree in applied mathematics, mathematical finance, engineering, or physics
The ability to set priorities to meet multiple deadlines with varying urgency
Creativity to tailor oral and written materials to differing audiences with a focus on delivering concise responses

Responsibilities: 

Develop and deploy risk and market analytics using our automated risk reporting system
Create Power BI reports to visualize and summarize analytical results and generate KPIs
Maintain and improve all aspects of the automated market risk system (Inputs, Code, Scripts, Queries, etc.)
Design, build, and test pricing formula, volatility curves, correlation matrix, VaR models, Scenario & sensitivity analysis
Direct improvements to our commodity trading and risk management system (CTRM)
Lead business process automation support project
Valuation of complex structured deals, asset optionality, and real options
Create ad-hoc models and reports while ensuring completeness and accuracy
Implement new metrics with respect to risk and its attribution

Location and other Key Details:

You will work out of our Calgary head office, located in the Suncor Energy Centre at 150 – 6th Ave S.W.
Hours of work are a regular 40-hour work week, Monday to Friday, with the potential for extended work hours based on business needs

The Growth and Performance Marketing team within Sun Life’s Client Experience Office (CXO) has embarked on a major transformation. As part of this transformation, we are continuously launching and testing new ideas, platforms, and solutions to generate new leads and identify opportunities for existing clients and group members.

As a senior data analyst on the Client Acquisition Analytics team, you will be part of a large analytics community and will be focused within the Growth and Performance Marketing business helping the team by, but not limited to, mining data for business insights, analyzing and interpreting trends using statistical tools and techniques, reporting on business performance, and triaging code and data-related issues.

You will be supporting several key initiatives that are tied to our vision of growing our client base, improving advisor lead conversion, supporting the Head Office lead Evolution program, monitoring of our key performance indicators and championing the Retail Leads Data Modernization.

To achieve this, we will be leveraging many systems across Sun Life, gathering requirements, engaging with subject matter experts, and creating reporting. All of this is to be able to tell the story of our clients’ journeys and gather insights to improve their experience.

What will you do?

Analytic work from requirements specification, data gathering, analysis of presentations to solve business problems.

Ongoing support to uncover opportunities that will drive incremental sales.
Develop metrics and KPIs to measure the performance of analytical and data products in the overall portfolio.
Provide support for annual business plan, monthly sales forecast, and insight analysis.
Operationalize reporting processes and synthesize key metrics into impactful and insightful dashboards to monitor and assess the success of the business initiatives/performance.
Perform reporting automation, self-serve analytics enablement, and promote the culture of analytics-driven decision making.

What do you need to succeed?

5 + years experience working with data (i.e., quantitative analysis experience, including handling, manipulating, and analyzing data, hypothesis testing, data modelling and data visualization)
5 + years experience with SQL. Comfortable writing accurate, efficient, but complex SQL queries to extract and integrate data from multiple database sources.
Experience of working with AWS data toolsets (eg: Glue, Redshift, SageMaker etc.) and knowledge of using Python/Pyspark
Experience using oral and written storytelling to share data driven insights in a clear, succinct manner.
Strong partnering approach with a commitment to meeting business partners' unique needs and expectations.
In-depth prioritization, planning, and change management skills to stay within time/scope of a task in a fast-paced environment.
Comfortable learning new applications and processes quickly with minimal direction
Ability to document work.

About the job
Position Description

CGI Edmonton is looking for a Data Analyst to support the data migration of a few legacy systems to a new cloud-based COTS solution. Additionally, there are data quality improvement requirements and migration requirements and there may be an opportunity to support the development of data-based enhancements (i.e., automate a reporting process).

Become a part of an outstanding culture that gives you the freedom to innovate, influence decisions, achieve your full potential, and chart your career. Our benefits include a share purchase program, profit sharing, wellness credits, training and development programs, and flexible work schedules).

Your future duties and responsibilities

 Support data migration from legacy systems to a new cloud-based COTS solution
 Identify opportunities for data quality improvements and enhancements
 Solve some of the most challenging and impactful problems using your data expertise, and ability to communicate compelling insight through data visualizations, reports, and dashboards
 Help create the platform, tools, and APIs necessary to enable other teams to work with data
 Efficiently handle vast amounts of data from multiple sources and destinations, including relational and NoSQL databases as well as external systems, both in batch processing and real-time delivery
 Work on high-priority initiatives using advanced analytics, predictive modeling, and data from a variety of data sources to produce actionable business insights
 Provide guidance to a customer and project team with respect to technical feasibility, complexity, and level of effort required to deliver a solution
 Work closely with other team members to further develop metrics, KPIs, and insights that measure business performance improvements
 Assist in the development and delivery of pre and post-sales POCs, presentations, and proposals for client engagements

Required Qualifications To Be Successful In This Role

 7-10 years of experience doing data analysis, data engineering, reporting, and advanced analytical modeling
 Hands-on experience in deploying reporting and analytical solutions to on-premise and cloud-based infrastructure
 5+ years of hands-on experience with Azure, SQL Server, DataFactory
 Hands-on experience with data reporting and visualization tools like Power BI, Tableau etc.
 Experience with modern software development techniques and methodologies: DevOps, Agile, etc.
 Knowledge and practice of secure software development processes

Desired Experience/Attributes:

 Experience with motor vehicle registry data
 Previous experience performing data migration is an asset
 Staying up to date with the latest technology trends and strongly desire to learn constantly.
 Highly detail-oriented with exceptional organizational and follow-through skills.
 Self-starter and able to execute without direction or oversight - demonstrable problem-solving skills.
 Value teamwork and urgency, with a passion for driving impact.
 Ability to handle multiple priorities and deadlines.
 Exceptional communication skills, with an ability to make technical concepts accessible and understandable to non-technical business users.

Education:

 Bachelor’s degree or diploma in mathematics, informatics, statistics, computer science, or information systems (or equivalent combination of skill and experience)

Job Summary

This position is a member of the Gas Market Analytics team, which is responsible for market analysis, maintaining and building fundamental market models, short- and long-term balance and price forecasting using statistical and qualitative methodologies in support of gas and power trading activities. Excellent opportunity including on the job training and exposure to working with many groups within the organization including Trading, Origination, Structuring, and Sales. The position will be responsible for owning the fundamentals of a region within North America, providing analysis and research related to the region’s natural gas markets, including coverage of adjacent energy markets impacting the region. These activities include both short- and long-term analytics, research, developing market views, and actionable trade strategies in support of Market Operations and Gas Trading activities as well as Corporate strategies. The Junior Analyst will have a focus on report automation, data visualization, building analytical toolsets, and data management in support of the Gas Market Analytics team.

Essential Duties/Responsibilities

Track fundamental drivers for the North American natural gas markets and develop methods of communicating this information to the Gas Market Analytics team and internal clients.
Assist in creation of proprietary views for the gas markets to provide internal clients with decision making information.
Incorporate data visualization techniques to revamp reporting capabilities and develop market analysis tools to aid in short term strategic decision making and tactical trading opportunities.
Advance data scraping and database capabilities with a focus on driving efficiency through automation of the reporting suite.
Process market intelligence and fundamentals to support and recommend front office trade and hedging strategies (short term - 3 years).
Operate and maintain simulation models to create short term and long-term balance and price forecasting for pipelines, storage facilities, and regional markets.
Disseminate daily market briefs and reports to the Commercial, Operations, Sales, and Origination teams.
Support groups across the company with natural gas intel, presentations, ad hoc analysis, and assist in providing Senior Management with materials for board meetings, earnings calls, investor day presentations, or other events as required.
Perform other duties as assigned.

Working Conditions

Open office environment.
Some overtime required as special projects arise.
Travel – minimal.
Hybrid: in-office and work from home

Minimum Requirements

Bachelor’s Degree in finance, Economics, Engineering, Statistics or related discipline from an accredited college or university (MBA/Masters preferred).
Strong analytical, mathematical, process modeling, presentation and report preparation skills and experience.
Proficiency with Excel required. 
Proficiency with at least one of the following tools: VBA, SQL tools, MATLAB, Python, R, Power BI

Preferred Qualifications

Natural gas experience a plus.
Base knowledge of the natural gas markets is a plus.
Excellent technical skills with proven ability to manage databases, perform web scraping, and leverage coding for report automation.

Additional Knowledge, Skills And Abilities

Effective oral and written communication skills, positive attitude and highly motivated. A self-starter, adaptive and versatile, able to work effectively in an active trading environment. Strategic, efficient, and entrepreneurial candidates will excel in this role. 
Able to prioritize tasks based on potential commercial impacts, able to meet aggressive deadlines.

Physical Requirements

n/a

About the job
Our client is looking to add a Sales Data Analyst to their Sales team for an Initial 6 month contract. In this role, the Sales Data Analyst will play a crucial role in analyzing extensive manual vendor reports, extracting pertinent data for billing downstream clients. Working within a manual process environment predominantly using Excel, the analyst will interpret data, allocate costs to clients, and collaborate closely with the finance team to ensure accurate billing for downstream clients. A keen understanding of billing cycles, vendor data, and billing concepts such as proration is essential for success in this role. 
This fully remote position presents an excellent opportunity for individuals with a passion for sales, data, and finance.

Qualifications:
2-4 years of experience in data analysis within sales, billing, or a technical environment 
Proficient in manipulating data in Excel 
Demonstrated willingness to engage in manual work, diving into details to ensure accuracy 
Effective communication skills, with the ability to thrive in a fast-paced environment

What will your typical day look like?

The role of Global People Analytics within Global Talent supports and/or leads projects as identified. The current portfolio is varied and changes often. The individual will identify data-driven insights for an executive audience, support experimental research for developing people analytics methodologies, and have experience conducting advanced data modeling and developing analytics solutions.

As part of the Global Talent team you will:

Manage the development and execution of advanced people analytics and data visualization in support of global, member firm or global business initiatives as needed, including strategic priorities
Support the design, development, and delivery of research experiments from planning, collecting, analyzing, and interpreting results
Develop compelling, logically structured, actionable data driven insights (including storytelling of research/analytics findings) for all audience levels, including Executives
Maintain and coordinate data collection, transfer, storage, analysis, and retention processes
Support the governance, execution, and coordination of data-driven strategic projects, analyses, and visualizations for Global Talent, and liaise with Deloitte Technology and Global Finance
Assist with preparation of deliverables (e.g., meeting agendas, presentations, summary/notes, etc.) for key project meetings (e.g. Deloitte People Analytics community) or Global Talent meetings (e.g., Executive Leadership Team) and leadership communications
Support management of ongoing relationship with key stakeholders associated with project and priorities
Collaborate on the development of tools and technology to support people analytics and the application of behavioral science
Support knowledge sharing across member firms and global businesses, including the delivery of special initiatives (e.g., working groups with MF stakeholders, developing internal points of view on talent topics, timely support on global issues like COVID-19)
Stay informed on new research and techniques related to people/HR analytics that could be applied to Global Talent priority areas
Future responsibilities could shift to other projects. If so, the underlying responsibilities would be similar, yet the topic area would change.

About the job
Cardinal Health Canada, with over 1300 employees nationwide, is an essential link in the Canadian healthcare supply chain, providing over 70,000 products to healthcare facilities and medical professionals across the country.
This is a contract position for 12 months, with hybrid work model. The Data & Analytics Function oversees the analytics lifecycle to identify, analyze and present relevant insights that drive business decisions and anticipate opportunities to achieve a competitive advantage. This function manages analytic data platforms, the access, design and implementation of reporting/business intelligence solutions, and the application of advanced quantitative modeling.
Data Analytics applies business process knowledge and data analytics to develop, recommend and communicate timely, accurate, relevant and actionable insights to support business decisions and objectives.
For more information on what it is like to work for us, please watch this video: Cardinal Health - Wings
Responsibilities
Transition existing Data Pipelines and reporting solutions into new Platform in the cloud
Design and build data pipelines that extract, transform, and load (ETL) data from various sources into our data warehouse
Create and maintain data models that ensure data consistency, accuracy, and accessibility
Develop and maintain automated data pipelines and data processing workflows
Create data visualization utilizing complex data to provide meaningful insights
Design and maintain databases that support our data processing and analytics needs
Ensure data security, privacy, and compliance with data regulations
Monitor and troubleshoot data pipelines to ensure data quality and reliability
Develop and maintain documentation for data infrastructure, processes, and workflows
Stay up-to-date with emerging trends and technologies in data engineering, machine learning, and automation
Qualifications
BA, BS or equivalent experience in related field preferred. Advance Degree may be required
4-8 years of experience in data analytics preferred
Proven experience in designing and implementing database solutions using SQL
Experience with cloud-based data platforms such as AWS or GCP
Intermediate level BI dashboarding experience (e.g. Tableau, PowerBI, etc.)
Knowledge of data modeling techniques and best practices
Strong problem-solving and analytical skills
Strong communication and presentation skills
Ability to work independently and as part of a team
Familiarity with SAP tables and data structures is preferred

How You’ll Make An Impact

Identify any data quality issues and partialities in data acquisition.
Coordinate with engineering teams to gather incremental new data.
Process, cleanse, and verify the integrity of data used for analysis.
Use data mining, model building, and other analytical techniques to develop customer segmentation.
Work with data scientists and leverage machine learning models that have been developed against Geotab’s big data environment.

Strong analytical skills with the ability to problem solve well-judged decisions.

Knowledge and experience with GHG emissions reporting, electric vehicle data and fuel efficiency practices are highly valued. 
Proven experience in data cleaning, with the ability to identify, analyze, and interpret inconsistencies or inaccuracies in data.
Strong critical thinking abilities, with experience leveraging data to make well-informed recommendations and decisions.

Our expectations:

Your role:

Generate and deliver comprehensive and accurate reports and create visually compelling dashboards using BI tools (e.g., Power BI)

Demonstrate proficiency in SQL, data warehousing, and ETL processes,

Translate business requirements into technical specifications for effective BI solutions.
Proactively identify opportunities for process improvement and optimization.
Provide leadership in the BI domain, offering guidance to junior analysts and team members.

Support design and implementation of data management and integration workflows, queries, automated on-line technical and business reporting, and other methods of providing content to users in a balanced and scalable manner from multiple data types and sources including a variety of technical data, information and content types including: GIS, IoT sensors, maps, geologic sections, photos/videos, vector models, remote sensing data, satellite imagery, environmental and social baseline, virtual reality, documents and relevant administrative and commercial data etc.
Collaborate with office, field and operations-based employees to understand business objectives and to provide guidance and advice for the efficient, appropriate and cost-effective management of project information throughout its lifecycle.
Support implementation of new data capture tools as appropriate maximizing mobile and cloud solutions where possible and appropriate to facilitate real-time coordinated data driven decision making.
Perform quality assurance on generated results to carry out data integrity and ensure metadata and spatial data standards are maintained.
Administer enterprise database systems for drilling and sampling (acQuire), spatial GIS content (ESRI), 3D modelling (Leapfrog Central) and other related content (SharePoint, etc) where applicable.
Assist with design and implementation of automated workflows, on-line technical and business reporting as required via the use of enterprise business intelligence tools.
Support the development of O365 standards and best practices to ensure effective and appropriate use of tools. 
Understand how to set goals and prioritize tasks in order to achieve business results.
Seek out and advises on trends in new technologies and best practices in GIS data management and makes recommendations on value added spatial initiatives.
Promote the company’s commitment to sustainability, the environment and health and safety, leads by example, and demonstrates honesty and sincerity and openness to feedback. 
Build a culture of teamwork across all constituents and stakeholders and encourages cooperation and open communication.
Foster a culture of open communication, focuses on building relationships across the organization and with external and internal partners, and invest in developing talent within the organization by providing recognition, challenge and mentorship.

Primary Purpose
Under the guidance of the Business Intelligence Analyst, the Junior Data Analyst ensures the integrity of the university’s enrolment management data through monitoring accuracy and participating in initiatives aimed at both streamlining data entry processes and improving overall efficacy as well as providing resources and support as required for data-entry staff to perform their jobs effectively. Additionally, they support the preparation of reports, presentations, and other documents that communicate data findings to various stakeholders.

Specific Responsibilities
Ensure the accuracy of data in the student management system by conducting regular audits to clean data, fill gaps, and reduce data disparity.
Identify issues in data entry processes that lead to errors, collaborating with appropriate staff and/or supervisors to address resolutions in a timely manner.
Support data entry staff and/or supervisors with queries regarding system issues, reporting needs, and/or questions.
Support the development and revision of reporting processes for increased automation and efficacy.
Facilitate the preparation of data-driven reports from multiple systems, summarizing and preparing the visualization of data.

*This job description outlines the key responsibilities for the role and is not meant to be exhaustive. Other responsibilities and tasks may be assigned or may naturally become a part of this role over time.

Job Details
CARFAX Canada is excited to announce the position of Senior Data Insights Analyst. In this role, you will work on-site from our London, ON office and report to the Director Data Insights and Governance. 
The Senior Data Insights Analyst will work closely with our Product, Data Acquisition, and Business Development teams to analyze the unique nature and value in new prospective data sources, validate business logic to increase our return on investment from the data we have and bring new fact-based perspectives to prove out new ideas.
The Senior Data Insights Analyst will possess strong Microsoft Azure experience including Azure Synapse, SQL, PowerBI, and emerging Microsoft tools to bring artificial intelligence and machine learning to the table in our analyses and to leverage productivity and effectiveness as we explore big data.
Position Responsibilities
Act as a subject matter expert with a thorough understanding of the data and its lineage.

The Opportunity

We're looking for a strong Master Data Analyst to support the Customer/Partner, Product, Vendor, and Contacts business domains. The role will focus on working alongside our business areas to provide solution support for the Master Data Management (MDM) program functionality. You must have data/master data experience, be used to working in ambiguous/complex programs, and have polished people and senior stakeholder engagement skills.

The Master Data Analyst will be responsible for assessing requirements, and designing and implementing successful Master Data Management solutions that comprise data cleansing, data ingestion pipelines, business process workflow, data matching & de-duplication, and standardization. You will work with a team to create a robust, sustainable, and flexible design and contribute towards technical delivery using a semi-agile delivery framework.

The Master Data Analyst should understand both technical and functional design and bring perspective from process, application, integration, data, technology, and security together into an overall solution design of Master Data Management capabilities.

You Are Great At

Approach: Responsible for applying MDM strategies, requirements, and policies aligned to the business vision, and leading MDM functional implementation 
Requirements: Plan and lead MDM requirement analysis sessions with business users and a thorough understanding of deterministic and probabilistic matching methodologies and master data hierarchy management
High-Level Design: Translate master data requirements into high-level design and oversee the delivery of functional components for master data solutions
Process: Responsible for the rationalization and management of master data across the full lifecycle, and accountable for MDM change processes
Partnership: Collaborate with key stakeholders to understand their environment with its opportunities and challenges to identify and drive fit-for-purpose solutions 
MDM Solution: Create enrichment solutions that include logic like validation, match and merge, and survivorship and perform data profiling, data scorecard development, exception management
Program Support: Develop, enhance, and support large-scale end-to-end MDM project implementation
Thought Leadership: Open to expressing and discussing ideas or issues with a range of technical stakeholders – such as leads, architects, and business/technical SMEs to drive best-in-class solutions
Data Quality: Provide guidance on Data Quality analysis on large and complex data sets
Data Governance: Collaborate with Data Governance team to design and build the policies in MDM
Data Transformation: Collaborate with Data Architects to design the data model and develop ETL flows for MDM solutions

What It Takes

At least 10 years of experience in leading MDM implementations
Well-versed with Data Enrichment (e.g. Dun & Bradstreet) 
Completed at least 3 full life cycle experiences in MDM/DG projects using any tools like Informatica
Strong in SQL and experience in Informatica MDM/DG and SAP MDM

Experience with high-level designs and overseeing the delivery of functional components for master data solutions

Position Overview:
The Business Intelligence Analyst will play a pivotal role in leveraging data to drive strategic business decisions for our client. The ideal candidate will possess a strong proficiency in Power BI, SQL, and Excel, demonstrating the ability to transform raw data into actionable insights. This role requires someone with previous experience in a similar business model within the wholesale distribution industry.

Key Responsibilities:
1. Data Analysis and Reporting:
- Extract, clean, and analyze data from the ERP system to generate insightful reports and dashboards using Power BI.
- Develop and maintain comprehensive and visually appealing reports for the business, highlighting key performance indicators (KPIs) and business trends.

2. SQL Expertise:
- Utilize SQL to query databases, conduct data validation, and perform data transformations to ensure accuracy and reliability of reports.

3. Excel Proficiency:
- Leverage advanced Excel functionalities for data analysis, modeling, and visualization to complement Power BI reporting.

4. Business Analysis and Requirements Gathering:
- Collaborate with stakeholders to understand business needs and gather requirements for reporting and analytics solutions.
- Conduct business analysis to identify opportunities for process improvement and efficiency.

5. Business Decision Support:
- Collaborate with cross-functional teams to understand business requirements and provide data-driven insights to guide decision-making processes.
- Identify opportunities for improvement and efficiency through data analysis, contributing to overall business growth.

6. Experience in Wholesale Distribution:
- Leverage previous experience in a similar business model within the wholesale distribution sector to understand industry-specific challenges and opportunities.

7. Data Governance and Quality:
- Implement and maintain data governance practices to ensure data integrity, accuracy, and security.
- Conduct regular audits to validate the quality of data and recommend improvements as needed.

Qualifications:
- Bachelor's degree in Business, Computer Science, Statistics, or a related field.
- Proven experience as a Business Intelligence Analyst, preferably in the wholesale distribution industry.
- Proficiency in Power BI, SQL, Excel, and business analysis is essential.
- Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
- Excellent communication skills to effectively convey insights and recommendations to non-technical stakeholders.
- Detail-oriented with a focus on data accuracy and completeness.

Opentext - The Information Company

As the Information Company, our mission at OpenText is to create software solutions and deliver services that redefine the future of digital. Be part of a winning team that leads the way in Enterprise Information Management.

The Opportunity

We're looking for a strong Master Data Analyst to support the Customer/Partner, Product, Vendor, and Contacts business domains. The role will focus on working alongside our business areas to provide solution support for the Master Data Management (MDM) program functionality. You must have data/master data experience, be used to working in ambiguous/complex programs, and have polished people and senior stakeholder engagement skills.

The Master Data Analyst will be responsible for assessing requirements, and designing and implementing successful Master Data Management solutions that comprise data cleansing, data ingestion pipelines, business process workflow, data matching & de-duplication, and standardization. You will work with a team to create a robust, sustainable, and flexible design and contribute towards technical delivery using a semi-agile delivery framework.

The Master Data Analyst should understand both technical and functional design and bring perspective from process, application, integration, data, technology, and security together into an overall solution design of Master Data Management capabilities.

You Are Great At

Approach: Responsible for applying MDM strategies, requirements, and policies aligned to the business vision, and leading MDM functional implementation 
Requirements: Plan and lead MDM requirement analysis sessions with business users and a thorough understanding of deterministic and probabilistic matching methodologies and master data hierarchy management
High-Level Design: Translate master data requirements into high-level design and oversee the delivery of functional components for master data solutions
Process: Responsible for the rationalization and management of master data across the full lifecycle, and accountable for MDM change processes
Partnership: Collaborate with key stakeholders to understand their environment with its opportunities and challenges to identify and drive fit-for-purpose solutions 
MDM Solution: Create enrichment solutions that include logic like validation, match and merge, and survivorship and perform data profiling, data scorecard development, exception management
Program Support: Develop, enhance, and support large-scale end-to-end MDM project implementation
Thought Leadership: Open to expressing and discussing ideas or issues with a range of technical stakeholders – such as leads, architects, and business/technical SMEs to drive best-in-class solutions
Data Quality: Provide guidance on Data Quality analysis on large and complex data sets
Data Governance: Collaborate with Data Governance team to design and build the policies in MDM
Data Transformation: Collaborate with Data Architects to design the data model and develop ETL flows for MDM solutions

What It Takes

At least 10 years of experience in leading MDM implementations
Well-versed with Data Enrichment (e.g. Dun & Bradstreet) 
Completed at least 3 full life cycle experiences in MDM/DG projects using any tools like Informatica
Strong in SQL and experience in Informatica MDM/DG and SAP MDM
Understand and assess sources to target map documents
Experience with business-facing activities such as gathering requirements, facilitating meetings, creating persuasive presentations, and the ability to prepare business-ready deliverables
Understand Governance and data harmonization concepts, practices, and their implementation
Experience of Agile and traditional SDLC delivery methodologies
Work independently, efficiently, and effectively under tight timelines to deliver results by critical deadlines
Experience with high-level designs and overseeing the delivery of functional components for master data solutions 
Excellent business communication skills and a collaborative approach
Strong analytical and problem-solving skills

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci.

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

About BBA

As a Senior Business Intelligence Analyst, your mission is to drive continuous product improvements by offering detailed operational support through reporting, deep dive analysis, and cross-functional collaboration. Based on your insights, you will help pinpoint the next growth of opportunities.

By proactively communicating with the right stakeholders, you help the team drive product improvement that creates real business value. You will work closely with our Marketing, Customer Success, Payments teams, Finance and Product Management as well as have an overall direct impact on the Company's success. 

This is a remote position with a preference for applicants in the Eastern Time Zone. 

The Senior Business Intelligence Analyst will be responsible for the following duties and obligations:

Responsibilities: 
· Improve and support operational effectiveness through developing metrics and reporting to assist in making data-driven decisions. 
· Build and maintain dashboards to help stakeholders easily understand the feature performance and the next growth opportunities.
· Present insights to senior leadership and contribute to guiding the organization in the right direction.
· Be proactive in doing deep dive analysis to provide actionable insights and measure the impacts.
· Monitor daily performance against key metrics to identify opportunities and anomalies. 
· Constantly review current operational processes and be a strategic partner in making recommendations for improvements. 
· Design and analyze A/B experiments to evaluate the impact of changes. 
· Stay relevant on industry trends and work with the product teams to develop high impact features. 
· Help define and shape companies' business intelligence products and tools. 

Qualifications and Requirements 
· 5+ years of experience in Data Analytics, Operations, or relevant work experience at a fast-growing tech company is preferred.
· Degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Math, Operations Research, Physics, Economics, or other quantitative fields.
· Experience with crypto, fintech, exchanges, wallets or other relevant financial services.
· Knowledge of (but preferred; experience in) AI and Machine Learning; Candidates should be able to analyze complex datasets, identify patterns, and make data-driven decisions using AI and ML methods.
· Methodical and experienced in data analysis, with a track record of guiding the organization toward improved decision-making.
· Experience building compelling dashboards using data visualization tools.
· Experience with JIRA and A/B tests is required.
· Fluent in Microsoft Excel and SQL. 
· Excellent communication skills in verbal and written English. 
· Excellent at communicating and presenting data insights. 
· Have a sense of ownership and assume end-to-end responsibility in your work. 
· Strong business acumen and data analysis ability to help stakeholders make data-driven decisions. 
· Ability to manage multiple competing priorities in a fast-paced environment. 
· Ability to work independently and as a self-starter; adaptable and able to react quickly to changing business needs.
· Ability to build collaborative relationships, results-driven and possess self-leadership skills.

Role Summary

As a Data Analyst for Payroll Implementation, your primary responsibility will be to analyze and interpret data related to the implementation of a new payroll system. You will work closely with the project team to gather and validate data, perform data cleansing and transformation, and provide insights and recommendations based on your analysis.

Key Responsibilities

 Collaborate with the project team to understand data requirements for the payroll system implementation.
 Gather, validate, and analyze data from various sources, ensuring data accuracy and completeness.
 Perform data cleansing and transformation to ensure data consistency and integrity.
 Develop and maintain data models, reports, and dashboards to visualize and present data analysis findings.
 Identify trends, patterns, and anomalies in data, and provide insights and recommendations to optimize payroll processes.
 Work closely with stakeholders to understand their data analysis needs and provide customized reports and analysis.
 Collaborate with IT teams to ensure data integration and migration from legacy systems to the new payroll system.
 Perform data validation and reconciliation to ensure data accuracy and consistency between different systems.
 Assist in the development and implementation of data quality control measures to ensure data integrity.
 Stay updated with industry best practices and trends in data analysis and implement them in the payroll implementation process.



Key Qualifications/Requirements

 Bachelor's degree in Data Science, Statistics, Computer Science, or a related field.
 Proven experience as a data analyst or similar role, preferably in the payroll domain.
 Strong proficiency in data analysis and visualization tools such as SQL, Excel, Power BI, or Tableau.
 Excellent data manipulation and data cleansing skills.
 Knowledge of database management systems, data warehousing, and data integration concepts.
 Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
 Ability to interpret complex data and present insights in a clear and concise manner.
 Strong attention to detail and accuracy in data analysis.
 Ability to work effectively in a team and collaborate with cross-functional stakeholders.
 Knowledge of payroll processes, systems, and compliance requirements is an asset.

Amazon Canada Fulfillment Services is hiring a Data Analyst to support the Inventory Control / Quality Assurance (ICQA) team. The Data Analyst assigned to ICQA will work closely with the ICQA and operations teams in Inbound and Outbound to provide data and analytical support for ACES initiatives, root cause investigation of defects, and will provide support to ensure compliance to ICQA-related SoX requirements.

The Data Analyst will own the insights, set up analysis, and create automated dashboards and reporting. They will be responsible for identifying data sources (internal / external) to invent and simplify mechanisms and create custom reporting and analytics automation tools. Operating in a fast-moving and sometimes ambiguous environment, you will be required to work autonomously, taking full control and responsibility for achieving business objectives. This role provides real opportunity to develop original ideas, approaches and solutions in an ever-changing and competitive business climate.

Key job responsibilities

 Development of data collection processes and data management systems
 Maintenance of data integrity (0% error rate)
 Designing of queries, compiling of data, and generation of reports in MS Excel
 Charting and graphing of data for reporting purposes
 In depth research of defect trends
 Data collection and entry as needed
 Data mining and problem solving
 Back up for Process Assistant duties

About the job
Opentext - The Information Company

As the Information Company, our mission at OpenText is to create software solutions and deliver services that redefine the future of digital. Be part of a winning team that leads the way in Enterprise Information Management.

The Opportunity

We're looking for a strong Master Data Analyst to support the Customer/Partner, Product, Vendor, and Contacts business domains. The role will focus on working alongside our business areas to provide solution support for the Master Data Management (MDM) program functionality. You must have data/master data experience, be used to working in ambiguous/complex programs, and have polished people and senior stakeholder engagement skills.

The Master Data Analyst will be responsible for assessing requirements, and designing and implementing successful Master Data Management solutions that comprise data cleansing, data ingestion pipelines, business process workflow, data matching & de-duplication, and standardization. You will work with a team to create a robust, sustainable, and flexible design and contribute towards technical delivery using a semi-agile delivery framework.

The Master Data Analyst should understand both technical and functional design and bring perspective from process, application, integration, data, technology, and security together into an overall solution design of Master Data Management capabilities.

You Are Great At

Approach: Responsible for applying MDM strategies, requirements, and policies aligned to the business vision, and leading MDM functional implementation 
Requirements: Plan and lead MDM requirement analysis sessions with business users and a thorough understanding of deterministic and probabilistic matching methodologies and master data hierarchy management
High-Level Design: Translate master data requirements into high-level design and oversee the delivery of functional components for master data solutions
Process: Responsible for the rationalization and management of master data across the full lifecycle, and accountable for MDM change processes
Partnership: Collaborate with key stakeholders to understand their environment with its opportunities and challenges to identify and drive fit-for-purpose solutions 
MDM Solution: Create enrichment solutions that include logic like validation, match and merge, and survivorship and perform data profiling, data scorecard development, exception management
Program Support: Develop, enhance, and support large-scale end-to-end MDM project implementation
Thought Leadership: Open to expressing and discussing ideas or issues with a range of technical stakeholders – such as leads, architects, and business/technical SMEs to drive best-in-class solutions
Data Quality: Provide guidance on Data Quality analysis on large and complex data sets
Data Governance: Collaborate with Data Governance team to design and build the policies in MDM
Data Transformation: Collaborate with Data Architects to design the data model and develop ETL flows for MDM solutions

What It Takes

At least 10 years of experience in leading MDM implementations
Well-versed with Data Enrichment (e.g. Dun & Bradstreet) 
Completed at least 3 full life cycle experiences in MDM/DG projects using any tools like Informatica
Strong in SQL and experience in Informatica MDM/DG and SAP MDM
Understand and assess sources to target map documents
Experience with business-facing activities such as gathering requirements, facilitating meetings, creating persuasive presentations, and the ability to prepare business-ready deliverables
Understand Governance and data harmonization concepts, practices, and their implementation
Experience of Agile and traditional SDLC delivery methodologies
Work independently, efficiently, and effectively under tight timelines to deliver results by critical deadlines
Experience with high-level designs and overseeing the delivery of functional components for master data solutions 
Excellent business communication skills and a collaborative approach
Strong analytical and problem-solving skills

OpenText's efforts to build an inclusive work environment go beyond simply complying with applicable laws. Our Employment Equity and Diversity Policy provides direction on maintaining a working environment that is inclusive of everyone, regardless of culture, national origin, race, color, gender, gender identification, sexual orientation, family status, age, veteran status, disability, religion, or other basis protected by applicable laws. Job Summary 
Reporting to the Senior Director of Digital Acquisitions, the Senior Data Analyst will play a pivotal role in the digital advertising strategy, focusing primarily on digital marketing opportunities across Paid Search, Social platforms and Affiliates. The Senior Data Analyst will lead and promote the implementation of advanced analytics and statistical methods to uncover insights and create dashboards that facilitate data-driven decision-making.
You are responsible for implementing best practices in advanced analytics for performance marketing, and will be working closely with the advertising channel leads, E-commerce, CRM and, tech teams for both brands GARAGE and DYNAMITE.
Primary Responsibilities
Analysis and operations
Perform in-depth analyses of large and diverse datasets to identify trends, patterns, correlations and provide actionable recommendations;
Build and own advertising tools and engine for Paid Media and Affiliates;
Use predictive modeling and rule-based algorithms to increase and optimize customer acquisition, engagement, revenue generation, and customer retention;
Business owner for the revenue attribution and multi-channel attribution analyses;
Develop processes and tools to monitor model performance and data accuracy; develop expertise in regards to the channels data integrations, automation and analytics.
Strategy: Thought partner ensuring data-driven decision-making
As the owner of revenue attribution, you will be responsible to follow technology roadmap that enables tracking and proper channel attribution, coordinate the conversations and decision-making in terms of steering marketing budget as a function of ROI for advertising dollars, marketing cross-channel efforts and media mix;
Understand business requirements and build optimization strategies that respond to different business targets (brands, geography, profitability, etc.);
Be a thought partner for the paid-channel marketing leads to ensure advertising budget is efficiently invested towards targeted performance;
Prioritize initiatives based on potential impact; create and execute the roadmaps.
Team and collaboration:
In close collaboration with the Senior Director of Digital Acquisitions and internal stakeholders (CRM and Loyalty, E-comm, Tech, Marketing, Finance, etc.), identify opportunities for leveraging company data to define business solutions in an iterative and collaborative manner, including collaboration with cross-functional teams to identify opportunities for GenAI applications and develop strategies for their effective use;
Provide guidance on best practices in data science, data synthetization, aggregation, testing, and measurement, and contribute to a collaborative and innovative work environment.

Qualifications:
Master’s degree in quantitative analysis fields such as BI, Machine Learning, Data Science, Mathematics, Computer Science, etc.;
Minimum 5 - 7 years of experience in a data science function, with a focus on driving business impact;
Strong knowledge of statistical methods such as regression, cohort analysis, hypothesis testing, cluster analysis, etc.;
Experience in E-commerce and/or digital marketing, or using data from digital advertising platforms (search, social media, affiliates);
Knowledge of modern visualization tools such as Power BI, Adobe Analytics, Tableau, Funnel, Datorama
Experience with data science tool sets: SQL, R, Python, Spark, Scala, SPSS or equivalent an asset;
Communicating clearly and regularly with teammates and stakeholders;
Understanding of web analytics an asset;
Interest in digital and emerging advertising platforms an asset;
Bilingual, excellent written English.
Over and above a competitive salary and bonus plan, registered retirement savings, and flexible group insurance with personalized coverage that meets your needs, you will be at the forefront of a growing organization that understands the importance of investing in people. You and your family can enjoy our employee discount at Garage and Dynamite, private sample sales throughout the year and many other exciting perks, including a very flexible vacation program.

ABOUT THE JOB:

Within Societe Generale Corporate & Investment Banking, the Global Markets Division brings together the Research, Investment and Risk Management Solutions, Execution and Clearing, Prime Services, Equities, Fixed Income, Futures and Currencies & Commodities structuring capabilities with the objective of providing investors with one integrated multi-asset market solutions team. The business uses an advisory and innovation mindset, focused on client needs, with a global leader in financial markets engineering. Global Markets is a leading player in derivatives, with unrivaled over the counter and listed derivatives expertise, as well as cross-asset and economic research. Our prime services' offering is a unique combination of execution, clearing, custody and financing services.

The Societe Generale Index (SGI) platform is responsible for the design, implementation and maintenance of systematic trading strategies for our client base. Using advanced mathematics and analytics, the team develops tailored made solutions that range from investment opportunities to hedging solutions.

SGI platform operates across Europe, Asia and Americas, with a regional focus and dedicated coverage that is integrated within the global ecosystem.

What will be your DAY-TO-DAY?

 Provide support to the daily production of AMER SGI scope encompassing accuracy of index calculation levels, client automated reporting and rebalancing execution.
 Work with traders, engineers and sales to address specific questions or requests around the cross-asset inventory.
 Contribute to the improvement of daily operations to achieve a robust SGI risk framework for the region.
 Implement standardized templates to streamline the creation and maintenance of the index, manage an intense launch lifecycle and ensure competitive time to market delivery.
 Implement and integrate quantitative metrics and controls into the broader SGI ecosystem to ensure a well-managed workflow and downstream dependency.
 Improve and maintain a consistent documentation of SGI platform, workflow, controls, and procedures.
 Partner with technology team and external data providers to integrate large scale datasets and develop data integrity checks for modelling daily ingestion.
 Participate to the design and building of a consolidated risk management tool providing customized risk views to engineering and trading teams, to better manage the inventory of SGI positions.
 Collaborate with trading, engineering, and sales teams to perform trend analysis, performance analytics and new design and solutions that will help trading, engineering and sales grow the franchise.
 Build-up the knowledge on the cross-asset SGI platform and navigate the transverse information system to conduct research & development, innovate and implement new optimized solutions.

 Profile required

Technical Skills

 Advanced quantitative and analytical skills.
 Skilled in programming using an Object-Oriented Language.

 Hands-on on quantitative analytics with ability to research problems and accompany them through established solutions.

We are a proud member of the Septodont group of companies. Septodont is a pharmaceutical and medical device company with a global leadership position in dental pain management. The group counts over 2000+ employees worldwide and has remained a 100% family-owned company for over 90 years. Our Cambridge facility serves as a significant manufacturing site within the Septodont group with high volume dental anesthetic production for a global customer base.

We have an opportunity for a Analytics Analyst/Developer.

Job Summary

The Analytics Analyst / Developer position works within our global data & analytics team – a group of engineers and data professionals who help Septodont improve our business by applying data science analytical methods. We are looking for candidates with a background and interest in business data analysis (applied to sales, marketing, and manufacturing), data science techniques, machine learning algorithms, and user-centric solution design. This is a junior role (seeking ~3 years practical work experience) and will be coached by our senior developers to help build their skills during initial projects.

This role is based at our Cambridge, Ontario location, and reports to the Director, Data & Analytics. The successful candidate will work with stakeholders remotely at our other locations, primarily USA and France.

Responsibilities

Apply business analytics & data science methods to help our stakeholders answer business questions.
Work collaboratively with business stakeholders to understand and translate business needs into solution requirements, prototypes, and operational solutions/systems.
Contribute to the analysis, design, build, test, deploy and support of data science solutions, preferably using our current technology stack (e.g., Microsoft Azure AI / Machine Learning, Python, Power BI).
Build data flows, models, and user-facing analytical tools which assist our internal business users to self-navigate our analysis outputs.
Contribute to the knowledgebase and working practices of the team, including our analytical approaches, delivery methods and artifacts, and processes.

Qualifications

Bachelor’s degree in computer science, mathematics, engineering, or related field or equivalent
3 years of work experience in an Analytics analyst or junior developer role (project experience building business analytics or reporting for use by internal company business teams)
Keen interest in AI/ML data science methods, demonstrated by initiative inside projects or another delf-directed research and development.

Experience & Interests

Data science methods as applied to business (sales, marketing, manufacturing, quality) – working knowledge of relevant machine learning and statistical algorithms.
Data flow development – primarily SQL based for structured datasets.
Data visualization methods and practices
Strong communication skills, with ability to interact directly with stakeholders across business units and accountability levels.
Proficient in English with excellent written and verbal communication skills. French is a nice to have.

What we offer

Excellent compensation/benefits package. 
Bonus and reward programs 
Discounted gym memberships 
Programs supporting work life balance. 
Employee recognition program 
Professional and personal development programs 
Social events and spirit days

What will your typical day look like?

The role of Global People Analytics within Global Talent supports and/or leads projects as identified. The current portfolio is varied and changes often. The individual will identify data-driven insights for an executive audience, support experimental research for developing people analytics methodologies, and have experience conducting advanced data modeling and developing analytics solutions.

As part of the Global Talent team you will:

Manage the development and execution of advanced people analytics and data visualization in support of global, member firm or global business initiatives as needed, including strategic priorities
Support the design, development, and delivery of research experiments from planning, collecting, analyzing, and interpreting results
Develop compelling, logically structured, actionable data driven insights (including storytelling of research/analytics findings) for all audience levels, including Executives
Maintain and coordinate data collection, transfer, storage, analysis, and retention processes
Support the governance, execution, and coordination of data-driven strategic projects, analyses, and visualizations for Global Talent, and liaise with Deloitte Technology and Global Finance
Assist with preparation of deliverables (e.g., meeting agendas, presentations, summary/notes, etc.) for key project meetings (e.g. Deloitte People Analytics community) or Global Talent meetings (e.g., Executive Leadership Team) and leadership communications
Support management of ongoing relationship with key stakeholders associated with project and priorities
Collaborate on the development of tools and technology to support people analytics and the application of behavioral science
Support knowledge sharing across member firms and global businesses, including the delivery of special initiatives (e.g., working groups with MF stakeholders, developing internal points of view on talent topics, timely support on global issues like COVID-19)
Stay informed on new research and techniques related to people/HR analytics that could be applied to Global Talent priority areas
Future responsibilities could shift to other projects. If so, the underlying responsibilities would be similar, yet the topic area would change.

 Analyste des données 

 Direction générale : Direction générale des ressources informationnelles et de la transformation numérique (DGRITN) 
 Direction générale adjointe : Direction générale adjointe de la gouvernance, de la sécurité informationnelle et de l’intelligence artificielle 
 Direction : Direction de la gouvernance des données et de l’intelligence artificielle (DGDIA) 
 Nombre d’emplois à pourvoir : 1

Étant un ministère qui œuvre partout sur le territoire et considérant la situation actuelle, nous avons l’opportunité de pourvoir cet emploi dans n’importe quelle région où il se trouve un bureau du ministère des Transports et la Mobilité durable

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci.

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

Ready to be part of the action?

Reporting to Senior Manager CDS, you will be responsible for efficient and effective managing and reporting of entitlement and mandatory corporate action related information with a high commitment to maintaining effective and cordial relationships with external and internal business contacts.

Key Accountabilities

Analyze all information pertaining to entitlement distributions and mandatory corporate action events for reporting pertinent information externally to CDS participants/subscribers and internally to various support departments.
Interact with Issuers/Legal Counsel, Transfer Agents/Paying Agents, DTCC and Securities Regulators, as deemed necessary, to validate information details and clarify any legal/tax implications of all entitlement distributions and mandatory corporate action events.
Ensure timely and accurate information reporting and distribution processing of entitlement and mandatory corporate action events through various systems and websites.
Summarize and prepare Depository bulletins, where applicable, detailing all relevant information for dissemination to CDS subscribers within the established service level standard.
Research and respond to all related queries/requests in a tactful, courteous and professional manner within reasonable timeframe ensuring customer satisfaction and resolution.
Exercise good judgment to promptly resolve and/or escalate problems/discrepancies within established timelines and document clearly all occurrences and exceptions for future reference.
Review procedures, guidelines and internal controls and recommend changes where appropriate ensuring operational excellence, risk mitigation and customer consideration.
Perform additional tasks as assigned from time to time to maintain effective coordination and management of the unit.

Must Haves

Post-secondary education in Commerce, Business Administration or Economics
Canadian Securities Course
3 years relevant experience in the financial/securities industry specifically in the Entitlement and Corporate Action operation areas.
Thorough understanding of security entitlement/corporate action procedures and depository operations including securities issuance and cancellation as well as DTC interface.
Excellent analytical/accounting skills to accurately determine complex entitlement payments and finalize corporate actions processes.
Strong organizational skills, ability to plan and prioritize regular tasks and special projects through to completion meeting strict deadlines in a time sensitive environment.
Excellent written and verbal communication, ability to write clearly and concisely and effectively interacts with external agencies through maintaining cordial relationships.

Fiche de poste - Analyste fonctionnel, Spécialisé en données

Chez Intelli5, nous sommes bien plus qu'une entreprise de technologies de l'information, nous sommes un catalyseur d'innovation en TI et d’excellence, tout particulièrement dans les domaines de la donnée et de l’IA.

Nous sommes aujourd’hui à la recherche de talents passionnés pour renforcer notre équipe.

Fondée en 2016 à Montréal, Intelli5 offre des services professionnels en TI aux entreprises situées au Canada et actives dans différents secteurs. Nous nous engageons à offrir à nos clients une approche entièrement personnalisée, une totale transparence et fiabilité. Nous croyons que faire le petit plus est ce qui fait la différence dans cette industrie compétitive. Nous prenons le temps de comprendre les objectifs et les défis de chacun de nos clients pour adapter notre offre de service afin de répondre et dépasser leurs attentes.

Nous investissons tout autant dans nos employés en vous offrant des opportunités de développement, des défis stimulants et un environnement propice à votre croissance professionnelle.

Rejoignez Intelli5 dans la suite de son aventure et faites partie d'une histoire de réussite en TI. Ensemble, nous pouvons accomplir l'extraordinaire.

Responsabilités
Agir spécialiste auprès des équipes de développement pour faciliter la transition d'entrepôts de données actuel vers Snowflake, puis ensuite participer à la mise en place d'outils de reporting. Il y aussi un volet de création de nouveaux entrepôts de données.
Participe à l'identification et à l’analyse des besoins d’affaires ainsi qu’à la définition des spécifications pour l’équipe de développement informationnel
Responsable de faire le pont entre le besoin du partenaire et l’équipe de développement
Peut être amené à participer à certaines preuves de concept à différents niveaux (modélisation de données, rapports Power BI, etc.)
Rédige et participe aux différents tests dans les divers environnements du produit informationnel (Dev, QA, Production).
Projet visant la modernisation et l’optimisation des processus d’affaires concernant la planification stratégique de la main d’œuvre.

Exigences
Avoir un minimum 6 ans d'expérience d'analyse fonctionnelle en intelligence d'affaires.
Avoir une connaissance des étapes par lesquelles passent les données, soit de l’ingestion jusqu’à la consommation, ainsi que des outils qui s’y rattachent.
Posséder de l'expérience avec le langage SQL et SSIS
Avoir une connaissance dans la réalisation de présentations à l’aide d’outils de visualisation de données, en particulier Power BI et MS SSIS
Avoir une connaissance de l’outil de développement Snowflake
