About Symcor

Symcor enables secure data exchanges and supporting business processes, to help clients succeed in an evolving digital world. Trusted by Canada's largest institutions for over 25 years to support their digital transformations, Symcor aligns industry participants to solve common challenges in the most effective and efficient way.

For more information, visit www.symcor.ca

 The Opportunity 

This position is an integral part of the Procurement and Vendor Management (VM) Team and will be responsible for data extraction and analysis, creating and updating reports on key performance metrics, spend actuals, forecasts and targets, collaborating with category managers and providing business intelligence to enhance data driven business decisions to achieve our goals. This role will also support sourcing events for supplier selection, drive contract management compliance and improve processes and data management within the space of procurement analytics.

This is a truly hybrid role with no mandatory days in office. We do request that the candidate is available to come in for a purpose such as in-person collaborations, team and company events, and as required based on team needs.

 About The Role: 

 Procurement Data and Spend Reporting. 
 Ensure Procurement Data Accuracy. 
 Vendor Management and Risk Management Data Reporting. 
 Optimize processes and data management within the procurement analytics space, identifying areas for improvement and implementing solutions. 
 Conduct regular reviews of procurement data to identify trends, anomalies, and opportunities for cost savings or process enhancements. 
 Communicate effectively with cross-functional teams, presenting complex data in a clear and concise manner to support decision-making at various levels. 
 Stay informed about industry trends, best practices, and emerging technologies in procurement analytics to continuously enhance the effectiveness of the role.

 Proficient in data extraction and analysis tools, such as SQL, Excel, Power BI as well as PowerPoint

Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, Americas (Remote CT/MT) 

About The Role

As a Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, you will support the CrowdStrike Sales and Executive Teams. You will work and support the CTO Labs and Field CTO Teams team at CrowdStrike. The Field CI team’s mission is to identify & deliver key competitive differentiators to support the international growth of customers, new markets, and TAM. This includes driving strategy through cross functional collaboration across the company including Product, Sales, Marketing, and more.

As the Field CI Analyst, you will be responsible for creating and communicating the company’s competitive differentiation strategy on a regional basis and working closely with the company’s product CTO’s, Product Managers and Field functions on a regular basis. You will also work closely with other groups within CrowdStrike, which includes: marketing, value management, legal and corporate affairs teams.

This role reports to the Manager, Competitive Intelligence Strategy. With your extensive cybersecurity background and your ability to think and operate at a strategic level, you will drive CrowdStrike’s technical vision and strategy and support on strategic engagements across the CrowdStrike organization.

What You'll Do

Support current customers and new customers by sharing CrowdStrike’s key competitive value differentiators, supporting the positioning of CrowdStrike as the leading thought leader for Cybersecurity with customers, partners, and analysts.
Driving and communicating CrowdStrike’s technology strategy to customers and partners as well as industry events.
Maintaining an in-depth knowledge of the cyber security industry, the competitive landscape and related industry developments to ensure we continue to be thought leaders who innovate ahead of the market.
Using stakeholders’ feedback to inform necessary improvements and adjustments to technology.
Focusing on technology improvements that will improve competitive positioning of the CrowdStrike products.
Providing recommendations for continuous improvement.

What You'll Need

Deep technical and operations skills in understanding the capabilities (strengths and weaknesses) of competitor offerings.
Strong analytical and communication skills to allow translation of competitive differentiation points into contextually relevant talking points.
Demonstrate a deep and broad knowledge of security issues and trends and are able to articulate a high-level security strategy to both technical and non-technical audiences.
Working in a role such as or similar to Competitive Strategist, Strategic Consultant, Enterprise Security Architect.
Experience with/exposure to Endpoint Security, Cloud Security, SIEM/Log Management, Mobile Security, Identity Security, Incident Response as well as other cyber security domains.
Regional travel is expected on a limited basis.

Benefits Of Working At CrowdStrike

Remote-first culture
Market leader in compensation and equity awards
Competitive vacation and flexible working arrangements 
Comprehensive and inclusive health benefits
Physical and mental wellness programs
Paid parental leave, including adoption 
A variety of professional development and mentorship opportunities
Offices with stocked kitchens when you need to fuel innovation and collaboration

We are committed to fostering a culture of belonging where everyone feels seen, heard, valued for who they are and empowered to succeed. Our approach to cultivating a diverse, equitable, and inclusive culture is rooted in listening, learning and collective action. By embracing the diversity of our people, we achieve our best work and fuel innovation - generating the best possible outcomes for our customers and the communities they serve.

CrowdStrike is committed to maintaining an environment of Equal Opportunity and Affirmative Action. If you need reasonable accommodation to access the information provided on this website, please contact Recruiting@crowdstrike.com , for further assistance.

The Position:
The Business Intelligence Analyst is a skilled analytical professional who has significant hands-on experience with analysis and reporting as they relate to the sales and marketing productivity in a large organization. As an Analyst, they will be responsible to create and develop metrics, see opportunities in the business and help shape the vision for reporting and analysis at OSL in support of client Samsung, Canada. 

Contract: 12 months. 

What you’re responsible for:
Responsible for creating and managing Power BI tools and has a thorough understanding of the BI system
Primary responsibility is to transform raw data into relevant insights via interactive and simple-to-understand dashboards and reports
Use Power BI to run DAX queries and functions. Create, test, and deploy Power BI scripts
Assimilate data from multi-dimensional databases to build weekly intelligence reports
Support the team with mining data, producing reports, dashboards and maintaining CMS
Assist in identifying opportunities in the business and works to produce impactful analysis
Examine reporting relationships to increase end-user productivity, availability and accuracy
Assist with the compilation and distribution of key financial and management reports
Liaise with internal and external clients on reporting needs to find effective solutions
Assist with new project opportunities to identify reporting and data system requirements
Utilize machine learning techniques and statistical analysis to identify opportunities

To be successful:
Proven working experience as a data analyst or business data analyst, writing Executive Level business intelligence reports
Technical expertise regarding data models, dashboard design development, data mining and segmentation techniques
Strong knowledge of and experience with reporting packages, databases (SQL, Power BI, MS Access etc) programming (Python, R, PHP, VBA and Java Script etc.)
Knowledge of statistics and techniques using statistical packages for analyzing datasets (ANOVA, f/t-Test, Pivot Tables, Power Query etc)
Knowledge of SaaS applications, SharePoint, MS Teams, CMS
Strong analytical skills with the ability to collect, organize, analyze, and disseminate significant amounts of information with attention to detail and accuracy
Adept at queries, report writing, data visualization and presenting findings using MS PowerPoint
BS in Economics, Computer Information Management, Statistics or IIBA Certified, Business Analysis Professional (CBAP) or related, an asset

To join our team:
Minimum five (5) years proven working experience in a reporting and analytics function
A Bachelor’s Degree in a related field such as business administration
Must possess the ability to proactively build strong relationships within a diverse organization
Must possess exceptional attention to detail and the ability to manage multiple on-going priorities
Superior organizational and planning skills are required
Excellent communication skills, both written and oral in English

What we offer:
A competitive base salary plus bonuses and other perks
Training and development opportunities to grow your career with one of Canada’s Best Managed Companies
A supportive workplace culture and work environment

What do we do?

It’s an exciting time to join Lumentum! Lumentum (NASDAQ: LITE) is a market-leading manufacturer of innovative optical and photonic products enabling optical networking and commercial laser customers worldwide. Lumentum’s optical components and subsystems are part of virtually every type of telecom, enterprise, and data center network. Lumentum’s commercial lasers enable advanced manufacturing techniques and diverse applications including next-generation 3D sensing capabilities. Lumentum is headquartered in San Jose, California with R&D, manufacturing, and sales offices worldwide. For more information, visit www.lumentum.com.

About the job
The Sr Analyst, Business Intelligence position will focus on supporting our clients by providing KPI and sales scorecards as well as insights and analysis to help support business initiatives. Incumbent must adapt well to quickly changing environments and collaborate effectively with other team members by sharing new and exciting discoveries related to discovery analysis and process improvements. This position entails working closely with our clients and leadership team to develop and implement retail and HQ reporting strategies. This is a client facing position with possible additional team / management lead responsibilities.

The incumbent(s) in this position should exhibit the following Acosta values:
People Minded – Must show dignity and respect to all people
Integrity – Must exemplify the highest degree of ethical behavior
Results Oriented – Must show passion, pride and commitment to succeed
Trust – Must be honest, sincere and confident
Teamwork – Must build trusting relationships
Innovation – Must progress through a combination of creativity, common sense and vision
Balance – Must maintain an optimistic attitude and keep perspective on what is important in life.

Essential Functions:
Support data-driven decisions to keep Clients’ competitive in the marketplace thru the utilization of the following data sources and tools. (POS data, Retail data, Shipment, Nielsen, Kantar, Etc.)
Develop and maintain client facing scorecards, measuring progress against defined KPIs. Provide visualization, analysis and next step recommendations.
Responsible for data accuracy- analysing data for completeness, format, and conformity.
Present data in clear and meaningful fashion, stay up to date on data visualization trends and theory. Required to interface directly with clients to present results and discuss KPIs.
Work closely with business and client managers to ensure quality results are delivered
Keep abreast of clients KPI's, strategies, innovation and other important information.
Participate in client meetings / QBRs to provide business analysis

About the job
POSITION OVERVIEW:

Navacord is looking for a Jr. Business Intelligence Analyst that can support business stakeholders’ to drive stronger results through faster decision making, management of risks, development of tailored product and services, market and portfolio expansion, and improved operational efficiencies. This role will pull and analyze large amounts of relevant data and translate that data into dashboards that effectively track performance, trends, patterns, and predictions
This individual should have an entrepreneurial spirit that encourages curiosity and innovation, data visualization skills, natural aptitude for tools as well as an analytical mind that supports problem - solving through data-driven solutions.

RESPONSIBILITIES:

Work with the Business Intelligence Team and stakeholders to design and build dashboard views that support overall strategic goals as well as monthly reports that communicate performance, trends/patterns, and predictions against those goals.
Mine large amounts of data from primary and secondary sources (BMS, insurer, market, etc.) that can be easily read by either human or machine, and support translating the findings into key insights to support the business.
Support the build and analysis of cross-platform marketing datasets to enhance stakeholders’ BI capabilities. Work closely with stakeholders to understand their needs and deliver solutions that automate and generate insights from their data.
Assist to Identify markets for future product development and methods to improve sales of existing products by analyzing technology trends.
Collaborate with the team to enhance sustainable analytic dashboards for better understanding of business performance, retention, growth and profitability.

ABOUT THE JOB:

Within Societe Generale Corporate & Investment Banking, the Global Markets Division brings together the Research, Investment and Risk Management Solutions, Execution and Clearing, Prime Services, Equities, Fixed Income, Futures and Currencies & Commodities structuring capabilities with the objective of providing investors with one integrated multi-asset market solutions team. The business uses an advisory and innovation mindset, focused on client needs, with a global leader in financial markets engineering. Global Markets is a leading player in derivatives, with unrivaled over the counter and listed derivatives expertise, as well as cross-asset and economic research. Our prime services' offering is a unique combination of execution, clearing, custody and financing services.

The Societe Generale Index (SGI) platform is responsible for the design, implementation and maintenance of systematic trading strategies for our client base. Using advanced mathematics and analytics, the team develops tailored made solutions that range from investment opportunities to hedging solutions.

SGI platform operates across Europe, Asia and Americas, with a regional focus and dedicated coverage that is integrated within the global ecosystem.

What will be your DAY-TO-DAY?

 Provide support to the daily production of AMER SGI scope encompassing accuracy of index calculation levels, client automated reporting and rebalancing execution.
 Work with traders, engineers and sales to address specific questions or requests around the cross-asset inventory.
 Contribute to the improvement of daily operations to achieve a robust SGI risk framework for the region.
 Implement standardized templates to streamline the creation and maintenance of the index, manage an intense launch lifecycle and ensure competitive time to market delivery.
 Implement and integrate quantitative metrics and controls into the broader SGI ecosystem to ensure a well-managed workflow and downstream dependency.
 Improve and maintain a consistent documentation of SGI platform, workflow, controls, and procedures.
 Partner with technology team and external data providers to integrate large scale datasets and develop data integrity checks for modelling daily ingestion.
 Participate to the design and building of a consolidated risk management tool providing customized risk views to engineering and trading teams, to better manage the inventory of SGI positions.
 Collaborate with trading, engineering, and sales teams to perform trend analysis, performance analytics and new design and solutions that will help trading, engineering and sales grow the franchise.
 Build-up the knowledge on the cross-asset SGI platform and navigate the transverse information system to conduct research & development, innovate and implement new optimized solutions.

Required

 Profile required

Skills and Qualifications:

Technical Skills

 Advanced quantitative and analytical skills.
 Skilled in programming using an Object-Oriented Language.
 Proficient in applied mathematics and modelling.
 Hands-on on quantitative analytics with ability to research problems and accompany them through established solutions.

Competencies & Qualifications: 

 Strong communication skills and ability to interface with key partners
 Good organizational and project management skills
 Preferably with an experience in systematic trading strategies
 Self-motivated with the ability to work within a team or alone as necessary.

 Analytical / Quantitative / Reactive and adaptive
 Data Science, Statistics and time series analysis skills is desired

Data Analyst Advisory

We are looking for an experienced Data Analyst to join our team.

Is this role right for you? In this role you will:

Communicate physical database designs to, and work with, database administrator to implement databases
Document data flows, identify appropriate data sources, entities, relationships and redundancies 
Manage data integrity and data quality. 
Maintain technical & business metadata. Generate metadata for Hadoop ingestion for different frameworks. 
Design data structures and document data meanings, definitions and intended use, work with various departments/leaders and data stewards to make the “metadata” available 
Define and document the data architecture for operational databases, reporting and provisioning platforms, including the physical components and their functionality
Support data strategies, standards, guidelines data quality process and governance across the enterprise
Provide leadership in researching and architecting emerging technology solutions to meet business objectives

Skills

Do you have the skills that will enable you to succeed in this role? We'd love to work with you if you have:

Relational and dimensional data modeling and database design, Erwin (Data modeling) skills.

Knowledge of data architectural approaches, patterns and emerging technologies (RDBMS, Hadoop and Cloud) 
Ability to translate business needs into technical solutions. Strong Analytical skills.
Experience creating architecture and strategy artifacts

Experience working in Agile environment

What will your typical day look like?

The role of Global People Analytics within Global Talent supports and/or leads projects as identified. The current portfolio is varied and changes often. The individual will identify data-driven insights for an executive audience, support experimental research for developing people analytics methodologies, and have experience conducting advanced data modeling and developing analytics solutions.

As part of the Global Talent team you will:

Manage the development and execution of advanced people analytics and data visualization in support of global, member firm or global business initiatives as needed, including strategic priorities
Support the design, development, and delivery of research experiments from planning, collecting, analyzing, and interpreting results
Develop compelling, logically structured, actionable data driven insights (including storytelling of research/analytics findings) for all audience levels, including Executives
Maintain and coordinate data collection, transfer, storage, analysis, and retention processes
Support the governance, execution, and coordination of data-driven strategic projects, analyses, and visualizations for Global Talent, and liaise with Deloitte Technology and Global Finance
Assist with preparation of deliverables (e.g., meeting agendas, presentations, summary/notes, etc.) for key project meetings (e.g. Deloitte People Analytics community) or Global Talent meetings (e.g., Executive Leadership Team) and leadership communications
Support management of ongoing relationship with key stakeholders associated with project and priorities
Collaborate on the development of tools and technology to support people analytics and the application of behavioral science
Support knowledge sharing across member firms and global businesses, including the delivery of special initiatives (e.g., working groups with MF stakeholders, developing internal points of view on talent topics, timely support on global issues like COVID-19)
Stay informed on new research and techniques related to people/HR analytics that could be applied to Global Talent priority areas
Future responsibilities could shift to other projects. If so, the underlying responsibilities would be similar, yet the topic area would change.

About the job
Flipp is a pre-IPO company on a mission to help shoppers provide for their families by making life more affordable by leveraging technology. We work with the largest retailers and manufacturers in the world to help them transform their businesses and connect them with millions of shoppers through our next-generation digital shopping marketplace. Our award-winning Flipp app is used by millions of shoppers every week to make better purchase decisions and to save 20-40% off their bills.

With the recent increase in costs of living, Flipp’s mission has never been more relevant. Flipp’s Shopper Consideration Platform allows retailers and manufacturers to create digital experiences from their savings & deals content. These experiences help Shoppers decide what to buy and where to buy it. Flipp then connects those retailer and manufacturer experiences to millions of shoppers through Flipp’s owned and operated channels.

As a Senior Partner Insights Analyst, you'll get the opportunity to act as a trusted advisor for our internal sales & product team members in support of our retail, brand and publisher partners. You'll leverage data & insights to drive strategy, formulate business actions and maximize demonstrated business results. You'll also communicate and coordinate plans with our internal sales and product teams to drive our business forward.

What You'll Get The Opportunity To Do

Execute and deliver against project timelines, such as data validation, analysis, and results
Perform test design, setup, execution & analysis (A/B testing, incremental lift, etc.) and provide expertise on testing, measurement, media mix modelling (MMM) and multi-touch attribution (MTA) both internally and externally to drive a meaningful revenue impact
Analyze historical data to understand trends in performance, and the impact of changes
Build and automate advanced queries to analyze data and optimize report solutions for efficiency (eg. SQL, Scala, Python, etc.)
Understand and define key requirements; communicate complex business and analytical concepts to internal Flipp team members, including senior sales team and product team members
Manage enterprise-level systems and large data sets for insight generation and analysis
Build and improve team knowledge base, sharing best practices, and case studies

What You'll Bring To The Team

2-3 years of experience managing projects cross-functionally; preferably applying analytics to business problems
Applied experience writing queries, scripts and stored procedures (eg. SQL, Scala, Python, etc.)
Experience with data visualization and reporting (eg. Thoughtspot, Tableau, Periscope, Domo, Amplitude, etc.)
Knowledge of various testing methodologies (A/B testing, incremental lift, etc.), media mix modelling (MMM), and multi-touch attribution (MTA) along with an understanding of how to apply them
A passion for constant improvement; always looking to do things better (both personally, as part of a team and for the company)
A quick learner, with an open-minded perspective to understand Flipp’s disciplined approach
Self-starter, highly effective working independently and within a team
Highly organized and great time management skills; ability to juggle multiple priorities at once
Understanding of the retail, CPG, loyalty, consumer analysis, and digital media domain is preferred

 The Opportunity 

Nova Scotia is undergoing an energy transition, with generation shifting to renewable sources and consumption patterns changing as more customers heat their homes with electricity and replace gas-powered cars with electric vehicles. As part of this transition, more detailed forecasts are required to predict not just how much energy will be used, but when and where. In order to help develop the analytic capabilities required for these changes in forecast methodology, we are currently looking for a Forecasting Data Analyst to join our Load and Revenue Forecasting Team in a permanent position. 

Key Elements Of This Role Include

Provide analysis of customer consumption data to support activities such as load and revenue forecasting, rate design, and cost of service. Data types include cross-sectional and time-series big data.
Collaborate within the load forecasting team and other teams in the development of an internal data warehouse, KPI reporting and dashboards using a variety of data visualization software, trend analysis and other ad-hoc reporting.
Design, build, and deploy collections of consumption data, and build models and visualizations that support multiple use cases across different domains.
Coordinate data collection and analysis activities for internal and external users.
Develop and maintain documentation of processes and procedures.

These Skills Will Make You Successful

To thrive in this role, you recognize yourself in most of the following competencies and skills listed below:

A Bachelor’s degree in Mathematics, Computer Science, Information Technology, Engineering or a related analytical field
Minimum of two (2) years in a professional data analytics role or equivalent.
Previous experience with data modeling or analysis in database systems, including programming and algorithm development
Experience analyzing large data sets to identify gaps and inconsistencies
Knowledge of statistical sampling techniques, regression, and time-series analysis
Experience with data visualization using Tableau and/or other visual analytics tools is required
Experience in the utility industry and understanding of electrical terminology is preferred
Capacity to work and communicate findings with a range of stakeholders, including superior written and verbal communication skills and an ability to clearly communicate complex technical concepts.

We understand that experience comes in many forms, and we’re dedicated to adding new perspectives to the team. So, if your experience is close to what we’ve listed above, please consider applying.

Starting Minimum Salary from: $ 66,300/year

Position Summary:

Reporting to the Operations Accounting Manager, the Data Control Analyst is responsible for responding to a high volume of incidents in ServiceNow. The Data Control Analyst will investigate and resolve data integrity issues raised by internal and external stakeholders by leveraging Parkland’s multiple data sources to determine the issue and proper method for correction with auditable workbooks and documentation. This role requires collaboration with groups internal and external to Order to Cash including AR Reconciliations, Hydro Carbon Accounting, IT, Settlements, and POS (Point of Sales), Retail Finance, and operations. Attention to detail and analytical mindset is critical to ensure that root cause analysis is performed and documented. At Parkland, Continuous Improvement is a core value, so this role will assist in the development of reports and automation using SQL, Power BI, with a working knowledge of Relational Databases.

Key Responsibilities:

Area specific: Data Control

Respond to and resolve incidents created in ServiceNow in accordance with our Service Level Agreement (SLA) ensuring auditable work and work notes.
Collect all documentation and approvals needed as part of the verification and correction process.
Update systems with accurate information, including ServiceNow, with auditable work notes and workbooks.
Collaborate with cross-functional teams to correct data in PDI (an Operating Platform) to ensure its’ accuracy so that Retailers are settled in an accurate and timely manner while protecting Parkland’s gross margins.

Trace la courbe de ta carrière dans l'équipe Innovation

Nous offrons un accompagnement technologique et des services techniques aux entreprises québécoises qui leur permettent d’innover et d’augmenter leur productivité de façon intelligente et durable. De plus, nos conseillers industriels accompagnent les entreprises dans l’identification et la priorisation de leurs besoins technologiques, les mettent en relation avec des ressources internes et externes et assurent le suivi des projets auprès des clients.

Le rôle: 

L’analyste en informations normatives et de marché est spécialisé dans le domaine des exigences normatives et de marchés pour les produits manufacturiers. Le titulaire doit, entre autres, accompagner les entreprises manufacturières qui souhaitent entreprendre un projet qui nécessite de connaître les exigences normatives des marchés d’exportations envisagés.

Les principales responsabilités: 

Analyser les besoins d’accompagnement des entreprises manufacturières en regard des aspects normatifs et de marchés d’un projet d’exportation et établir une proposition d’accompagnement;
Étudier les caractéristiques techniques des produits manufacturiers visés par un projet d’exportation;
Collecter, analyser et synthétiser des données normatives et de marchés afin de produire une information à valeur ajoutée en regard de chaque produit manufacturier étudié;
Répondre aux demandes d’informations techniques des entreprises en les orientant vers des normes, lois et règlements touchant leurs produits manufacturiers, tant pour le Canada que pour d’autres pays;
Produire des rapports, des bulletins, des conclusions et/ou des réponses, les livrer et en assurer la présentation et le suivi auprès des entreprises;
Effectuer la gestion de projets d’accompagnement;
Réaliser des présentations/conférences/formations en lien avec les aspects normatifs de l’exportation et/ou l’acceptation de produits;
Maintenir à jour ses connaissances au niveau des normes, lois et règlements touchant les secteurs manufacturiers canadiens et étrangers;
Entretenir et développer des relations d’affaires avec les organismes normatifs, les laboratoires canadiens et étrangers et des intervenants/experts dans les différents marchés d’exportation;
Accomplir, au besoin, toute autre tâche nécessaire au bon fonctionnement de l’organisation.

Baccalauréat en génie mécanique ou dans une discipline connexe
Posséder au minimum trois ans d’expérience et des connaissances en rapport direct avec la conformité de produits, les normes, les procédures et la réglementation internationale en matière d’exportation;
Avoir des connaissances et de l’expertise reliées à l’analyse de quantité importante de documents;
Avoir une bonne connaissance des plateformes informationnelles, des agents intelligents et des moteurs de recherche;
Avoir une bonne connaissance de la suite Microsoft Office;
Avoir une excellente connaissance du français et de l’anglais tant à l’oral qu’à l’écrit;
Être disponible pour des déplacements au Québec

Le profil général recherché:

Être orienté vers le client.
Posséder d’excellentes habiletés de recherche, d’analyse, de synthèse et de vulgarisation de données multiples.
Faire preuve d’autonomie et de dynamisme
Démontrer des aptitudes au travail d’équipe
Être à l’aise de s’exprimer en public. 

Le salaire: 51 692$ à 95 747 $

Investissement Québec t’offre plusieurs avantages

Connecte avec tes collègues : Travaille de la maison jusqu’à trois jours par semaine et profite de l’énergie du bureau pour créer, t’inspirer, collaborer et avoir du plaisir! Plusieurs formules d’horaires flexibles te permettant de mieux concilier vie personnelle et professionnelle, tout en respectant ton profil d’emploi.

Allonge tes journées de travail pendant quatre jours pour obtenir une demi-journée de congé.
Évite le trafic en réalisant tes 7 heures de travail entre 7 h 30 et 18 h.
Profite de congés payés un vendredi après-midi sur deux durant l’été
Bénéficie de 2 semaines complètes en télétravail au Québec par année 

Dépasse-toi : Plusieurs options te sont offertes pour parfaire tes connaissances, améliorer tes compétences professionnelles ou tes habiletés de gestion. S’ajoutent à cela des congés pour études, le remboursement des frais pour l’obtention d’une attestation professionnelle, le remboursement de matériel de cours, et encore plus.

Prends soin de ta santé : Nous offrons des services de télémédecine tout à fait gratuitement. Notre programme de santé-mieux-être TonIQ, te permet également de profiter de conférences et de suggestions d’activités favorisant un bel équilibre de vie.

Reste actif : Nous remboursons une partie des frais d’inscription à ton programme de santé physique.

Sens-toi soutenu en toutes circonstances : Notre programme d’aide aux employés et à la famille t’apporte un soutien gratuit, immédiat et confidentiel.

Réalise-toi maintenant et prépare ton avenir en même temps! Nos employés adhèrent automatiquement à notre régime de retraite à prestations déterminées, l’un des plus généreux de notre secteur d’activité.

Sois rassuré, tu seras assuré: Nous offrons un régime d’assurances collectives flexibles pouvant être modulés en fonction des besoins (selon admissibilité).

 Vois la vie en vert: Plusieurs initiatives en développement durable s’ajoutent à notre bilan chaque année : remboursement d’une partie de tes titres de transport, stationnement à vélos gratuit, distributrices à eau pour éviter le gaspillage de plastique.
About the job
Renseignements généraux

Vous avez envie d’action ? De travailler au sein d’une équipe dynamique ? De participer à l’amélioration de la qualité de vie des Québécoises et des Québécois ? Saisissez cette occasion de mettre de l’avant votre implication et votre créativité afin de faire concrètement la différence. Le ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable (le Ministère) vous offre notamment un milieu de vie qui privilégie de nouvelles pratiques de gestion audacieuses et mieux adaptées aux réalités de la nouvelle génération. Grâce à l’approche Entreprise en santé, le Ministère est soucieux de la qualité de vie au travail de son personnel et désire offrir un milieu collaboratif, mobilisateur et respectueux, qui favorise la santé et le mieux-être des personnes. Laissez-vous transporter vers de nouveaux défis et joignez-vous au ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable !

Vous êtes à la recherche d’une opportunité exceptionnelle pour développer votre carrière et vous aimeriez contribuer à l’essor de l’intelligence artificielle dans le domaine des transports ? Rejoignez-nous aujourd’hui et faites partie d’une équipe passionnée qui écrira une nouvelle page de l’ère numérique!

 Analyste des données 

 Direction générale : Direction générale des ressources informationnelles et de la transformation numérique (DGRITN) 
 Direction générale adjointe : Direction générale adjointe de la gouvernance, de la sécurité informationnelle et de l’intelligence artificielle 
 Direction : Direction de la gouvernance des données et de l’intelligence artificielle (DGDIA) 
 Nombre d’emplois à pourvoir : 1 
 Statut de l’emploi : Régulier 
 Lieu de travail : 900 boulevard René-Lévesque Est, Québec* 
 Télétravail : en mode hybride 
 Horaire de travail : 35 heures par semaine 
 Date prévue d’entrée en fonction : Février 2024 
Étant un ministère qui œuvre partout sur le territoire et considérant la situation actuelle, nous avons l’opportunité de pourvoir cet emploi dans n’importe quelle région où il se trouve un bureau du ministère des Transports et la Mobilité durable

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci. 

 Les avantages de travailler au ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable 

 Régime de retraite à prestations déterminées avantageux ; 
 Régime d’assurances collectives ; 
 20 jours de vacances après seulement un an de service et 13 jours fériés ; 
 Mesures de conciliation travail et vie personnelle ; 
 Horaire variable ; 
 Sécurité d’emploi ; 
 Programme d’aide aux employés (PAE) ; 
 Programme de soutien aux études ; 
 Service de formation et de développement au sein de l’organisation ; 
 Soutien financier à la pratique d’activités physiques. 

 Salaire annuel : 

51 776 $ à 90 110 $ selon l’expérience

L’échelle salariale peut être consultée sur le site Web du Secrétariat du Conseil du trésor . À l’embauche, l’échelon sera déterminé en fonction de l’expérience du candidat.

La rémunération est déterminée en fonction de la pertinence de votre scolarité et de vos expériences en lien avec l’emploi. Par conséquent, il est important de bien les détailler dans votre formulaire d’inscription qui servira de référence.

Profil recherché

 Les qualités que nous recherchons : 

 S’adapter facilement aux changements et aimer le travail en équipe ; 
 Faire preuve d’autonomie, de créativité et d’initiative ; 
 Démontrer un excellent sens de l’organisation et une grande rigueur ; 
 Posséder une excellente connaissance de la langue française parlée et écrite. 

 La personne recherchée doit satisfaire aux exigences de l’emploi : 

 Détenir un diplôme universitaire de premier cycle dans le domaine de l’informatique, de l’administration ou dans un domaine jugé pertinent dont l’obtention requiert un minimum de 90 crédits ou une attestation d’études pertinentes dont l’équivalence est reconnue par l’autorité compétente. 1 

La candidature d’une personne qui est en voie de terminer la dernière année de scolarité exigée pour l’obtention du diplôme requis pourrait être considérée.

Chaque année de scolarité manquante peut être compensée par une année de scolarité pertinente de niveau égal ou supérieur à celle exigée. Le diplôme exigé peut également être compensé par une maîtrise dans une discipline pertinente comportant un minimum de 45 crédits.

 Posséder au moins une (1) année d’expérience comme analyste des données. 
 Avoir une connaissance du français appropriée aux fonctions ; 
 Posséder la citoyenneté canadienne, le statut de résident permanent ou un permis de travail émis par l’autorité fédérale compétente pour occuper un emploi dans la fonction publique du Québec². 

 Autres éléments du profil recherché : 

 Connaitre l’environnement informationnel et l’intelligence d’affaires en soutien aux besoins stratégiques, tactiques et opérationnels ; 
 Connaitre les outils d’analyse et d’exploitation des données pour des fins de production d’information, notamment : SQL de Oracle, Oracle PL/SQL, PostegreSQL, Microsoft PowerPivot, Power BI, Oracle Discoverer, Python/R et SSRS ; 

Ce ou ces postes sont à pourvoir dans la ou les villes suivantes : Toutes les régions du Québec

 Détailler votre scolarité ; 
 Détailler vos expériences de travail, notamment en inscrivant votre emploi actuel et vos emplois antérieurs ; 
 Indiquer, à l’aide du menu déroulant de la section « Exigences et atouts », si vous détenez les exigences de l’emploi et atouts spécifiques indiqués à la section « Profil recherché » (si applicable). C’est notamment avec cette information que les candidatures répondant le mieux au profil recherché seront repérées. Lorsque vous aurez soumis votre candidature, les informations contenues dans le formulaire ne pourront plus être modifiées ; 
 Joindre toutes les pièces justificatives appuyant votre candidature. 

 Aucun curriculum vitae n’est accepté ni aucune candidature transmise par courriel. 

 Veuillez noter que seules les personnes retenues pour une entrevue seront contactées.

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

Visitez notre site Web Emplois au Quebec.ca/emplois-transports

About The Role

We are seeking a passionate competitive intelligence/field professional to support our product and sales teams. This role will function as the competitive product leader within CrowdStrike for Falcon for IT.

In this role you will be directly working with our product teams to guide roadmap decisions by developing a deep, nuanced understanding of the competition’s technical capabilities, primary GTM strategy/tactics, as well as why CrowdStrike wins or loses vs. the competition in visibility and automation in IT and security workflows. You will partner with senior leaders across Product Groups, Sales, Enablement, and Marketing to achieve these objectives and scale to a global level.

This role requires deep technical knowledge in IT cyber security, and a functional understanding of actual real-world deployments, extended use-cases, and customer motivations. Make recommendations on sales tactics and product strategy to enable CrowdStrike to win in the market.

This is an individual contributor, remote work position.

What You’ll Do

You will be required to synthesize and formulate guidance from a variety of information levels and sources (technical, business, field, external) and regularly present key takeaways to the field and to senior leadership
Provide a field-actionable, in-depth and ever-evolving understanding and analysis of the IT Operations (IT Ops) visibility and automation market relative to CrowdStrike solutions and capabilities
Provide tailored deal support (competitive surgeries & guidance), and develop a deep rapport with the field
You will work closely with the rest of the Competitive Intelligence team at CrowdStrike, as well as other key stakeholders (including the office of the CTO, field leadership, sales ops, product, and marketing teams), functioning as a primary liaison for IT Ops competition which includes development of competitive support material and competitive readiness plans
Make recommendations on sales tactics and product strategy to enable CrowdStrike to win in the market
Will be expected to be a self-starter with an ownership mentality. You will work autonomously in the development of project plans, requirements, timelines, content, and ongoing tracking/updates of the IT competitive landscape.

What You’ll Need

Bachelor’s degree or higher in a relevant field
Minimum 5 years of experience in the IT market with heavy emphasis on IT Ops and endpoint management
Minimum of 5 years relevant work experience (Ideal candidates will have experience in at least TWO of the following): sales engineer/pre-sales, competitive intelligence, solution architect, sales operations, product management, technical marketing, professional services, and technical support
Proven ability to synthesize complex technical concepts into field actionable guidance and executive summaries
Superior communication skills including experience presenting to senior & executive level management
Excellent people and project management skills to manage projects and interact/build rapport with staff, colleagues, cross-functional teams and third parties

Bonus Points

Direct experience with customers (as a customer, or in a customer support or field role)
Hands-on experience with products (either evaluating/testing or in production)

Benefits Of Working At CrowdStrike

Remote-first culture
Market leader in compensation and equity awards
Competitive vacation and flexible working arrangements 
Comprehensive and inclusive health benefits
Physical and mental wellness programs
Paid parental leave, including adoption 
A variety of professional development and mentorship opportunities
Offices with stocked kitchens when you need to fuel innovation and collaboration

We are committed to fostering a culture of belonging where everyone feels seen, heard, valued for who they are and empowered to succeed. Our approach to cultivating a diverse, equitable, and inclusive culture is rooted in listening, learning and collective action. By embracing the diversity of our people, we achieve our best work and fuel innovation - generating the best possible outcomes for our customers and the communities they serve.

What You’ll Do

Work closely with the Capital Markets team to evaluate, structure and price consumer asset-backed transactions
Develop and enhance capital structuring and pricing models tailored to Affirm’s consumer loan portfolio to enable efficient deal execution
Build quantitative models to analyze and predict the performance of Affirm’s consumer loans
Provide insights on capital markets deals to cross-functional teams for more optimal and efficient funding strategy and merchant pricing
Partner cross-functionally with our Capital Markets, Treasury, Merchant Pricing, Credit, Commercial, Product and Engineering teams to evaluate funding, product, and business decisions

What We Look For

4+ years of relevant experience structuring asset-backed transactions, forecasting consumer loan performance, and/or building quantitative models
Experience with industry-standard tools such as Intex/Bloomberg and working with accountants, rating agencies, and internal/external partners
Experience with SQL, Python, or other scripting languages
Strong interpersonal and communication skills, and ability to collaborate and influence across different teams in the organization
A proactive leader that can seek out new opportunities, drive projects, navigate ambiguity and develop creative solutions with minimal guidance
Desire to understand the broader context of business decisions

About Agoda

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 3.6 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

THIS ROLE IS BASED IN BANGKOK, THAILAND (WITH RELOCATION PROVIDED)

Location: Bangkok, Thailand (*Not open for remote work.)

Get to Know our Team:

As part of the Supply Analytics, you will be responsible for identifying new partners and opportunities, cultivating a relationship with them, and working together with them to deliver the best outcome for our end customers. You would also be responsible with managing the day-to-day interaction with the partner and working closely with other teams within Agoda to ensure the partners needs are met.

Description

Allucent is a full-service contract research and development organization with international resources dedicated to helping pharmaceutical and biotechnology companies efficiently and expeditiously navigate the regulatory approval process in order to bring new drugs, biologics, and medical devices to the people who need them. Allucent is a non-laboratory environment. At Allucent, our mission is to help bring new therapies to light. When you work at Allucent, that means rolling up your sleeves and applying your scientific knowledge, clinical expertise, and experience to partnerships with our clients in small and mid-sized biotech companies.

These customers have new therapeutic ideas, but want a partner who can assist with the clinical trial process, the complexities of certain disease states, or other critical capacities. You’ll work with them on the newest treatment breakthroughs for some of the most perplexing conditions. And ultimately, you’ll help make a positive difference in patients’ lives.

We are looking for an experienced Principal Biostatistician to join our Team in the United States OR Canada.

Summary:

The Principal Biostatistician (PrBios) supports the statistical analysis and clinical data activities of the Allucent Biostatistics/Statistical Programming team. This position leads projects, writes statistical documents and statistical sections of study documents for studies of all complexity, and provides senior review of statistical documents and outputs. This position may assist in the programming of datasets and outputs using SAS®. The PrBios will regularly interact with other members of the Allucent biostatistics project team and will interact with clients when leading a study.

This is a full-time, direct hire opportunity for an experienced Biostatistician Professional residing in the USA. Ideal candidates should have a strong CRO background with the ability to independently lead projects of moderate and high complexity as the lead biostatistician.

This position will be hybrid for those living near one of our office locations, however, for those further in distance the role can be offered remotely. Strong English Communication (written and verbal) is required.

Key Responsibilities:

Prepare statistical analysis plans (SAPs) and table, listing, and figure (TLF) mocks for a study of any complexity
Remain familiar with complex statistical methods and concepts in clinical research with emphasis in the development & support of the analysis of clinical trials. 
Provide senior reviews of statistical documents, data, and outputs for studies of all complexity to ensure quality and integrity
Execute a statistical analysis of any complexity as specified in a protocol or analysis plan
Interpret and communicate results for complex statistical analyses and outputs
Develop and/or review the statistical sections of a study protocol or clinical study report for studies of any complexity level, ensuring accurate descriptions of statistical methods used
Provide randomization materials including randomization schedules and treatment kit lists per Allucent SOPs and the sponsor-approved specifications
Develop or review documents for integrated analyses (e.g. ISS/ISE), including integrated SAPs and statistical sections of integrated study reports
Provide input and support responses to regulatory questions on statistical issues relating to client regulatory submissions
Maintain working knowledge CDISC standards and SAS® for production and validation of datasets & statistical outputs
Write and review specifications for complex ADaM or analysis datasets
Annotate or review annotations of TLF mocks to assist programming efforts
Review CRF design to ensure it conforms with the study protocol and analysis needs
Review data management documents as requested to ensure integrity of study data
Lead highly complex projects by fulfilling the following responsibilities: communicate with the client and statistical team, set and achieve timelines and milestones, ensure proper execution of the study SAP, monitor programming efforts in collaboration with the lead programmer, and work with management to ensure adequate resourcing
Lead management of project budgets, the identification of out-of-scope work, and the change order process
Function as the lead unblinded statistician for studies and manage unblinded tasks including implementation of interim analyses and participation in DMC/safety review meetings
Lead biostatistics and programming activities for a program of studies of high complexity and/or of high value. 
Support staff learning & development within the company 
Identify, recommend, and execute departmental initiatives, tools, and process solutions to enhance efficiency and quality
Provide mentoring to junior staff
Understand and comply with all company policies and SOPs
Review and evaluate biostatistics and statistical programming processes and procedures within the Quality Management System 
Represent Allucent at proposal bid defenses and/or marketing meetings with prospective clients
Support in preparation of new proposals
Establish positive relationships with current and future clients
Maintain strong long-lasting relationships to win new and repeat business
Contribute to other areas of business as required 

Requirements

Graduate degree (Master’s degree/local equivalent, or higher) in a relevant discipline including, but not limited to, statistics, mathematics, life science, epidemiology or healthcare 
Minimum 8 years of relevant work experience
Good knowledge of GxP and knowledge of SAS
Strong familiarity with relevant regulations and guidelines
GDPR/HIPPA, CFR/CTR/CTD and applicable (local) regulatory requirements
Working knowledge of computer systems, applications and operating systems
Demonstration of critical thinking and analytic skills
Strong written and verbal communication skills including good command of English language 
Ability to work in a fast-paced challenging environment of a growing company
Strong individual initiative 
Excellent attention to detail and commitment to quality
Proficiency with various computer applications such as Word, Excel, and PowerPoint
Ability to establish and maintain effective working relationships with co-workers, managers, clients, and vendors
Collaborative abilities and client focused
 Ability to effectively manage multiple tasks and projects
 Strong leadership skills
 Effective at problem solving, strategic thinking and conflict resolution

Position Summary

ILI MFL Data Analyst II performs all analysis activities including data setup, data searches, feature detection and identification. Assist in training data analysis personnel enabling progression through defined competence levels.
Performs other assigned tasks.

Étant un ministère qui œuvre partout sur le territoire et considérant la situation actuelle, nous avons l’opportunité de pourvoir cet emploi dans n’importe quelle région où il se trouve un bureau du ministère des Transports et la Mobilité durable

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci.

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

About the job
The Senior Biostatistician serves a lead role on projects. He/she interacts with team members in designing and analyzing clinical trials. Key responsibilities and skills include, but are not limited to:

Responsible for protocol development including study design, sample size estimation, randomization, and statistical analysis plan for assigned studies.
Provide statistical oversight to studies and assure adequate quality and consistency with project requirements.
Responsible for accuracy and completeness of database quality checks.
Responsible for assuring that data for statistical analyses are complete, accurate and consistent.
Responsible for statistical analysis plans and the accuracy and timeliness of statistical input into reports or decisions.
Responsible for validity of analysis and alternative analysis strategies when unforeseen circumstances arise.
Demonstrates extensive understanding of statistical concepts and methodologies. Recognizes and corrects flaws in scientific reasoning and statistical interpretation.
Responsible for accuracy and consistency of statistical tables, figures, and data listings, accuracy of report text, and consistency between summary tables in the body of reports and the corresponding source tables and listings.
Responsible for statistical methods section for the reports. Identifies and corrects flaws in interpretation of results, inconsistency in presentation or inference, adherence to the report guidelines, and assures project-wide consistency.
Effectively mentor non-statistical peers with regards to statistical methodology and provide appropriate background, motivation, and training to junior statisticians.
Effectively coordinate assignments and review deliverables so that projects are delivered on time with high quality.


Requirements:

MS or PhD in Statistics, Biostatistics or related field. Ph.D. with 2+ years of experience or MS with 4+ years of experience.
High degree of technical competence and communication skill, both oral and written.
Competent in experimental design, descriptive and inferential statistics.
Pharmaceutical, CRO, or related industry experience with clinical trials.

 Vos missions au quotidien

À PROPOS DU POSTE :

Au sein de la Banque d’Affaires et d’Investissement de la Société Générale, la division Marchés Globaux regroupe la recherche, les solutions d’investissement et de gestion des risques, la négociation et règlement de transactions, les services de garde de valeur, pour les actions, obligations, contrats à terme, devises, commodités ainsi que capacités de structurations dans le but de fournir aux investisseurs une plate-forme globale à multiple classes d’actif. Notre activité repose non seulement sur une approche consultative axée sur l’innovation, mais également centrée sur les besoins des clients. La division des Marchés Globaux est un acteur majeur dans les produits dérivés listés et de gré-à-gré mais aussi à travers les différentes classes d’actif ainsi qu’en macro-économie. Notre offre de service en compensation et garde de valeur offre une combinaison unique en ce qui a trait au transactionnel des marchés, compensation des produits dérivés, gardien de valeur et services de financement.

Société Générale Index (SGI) platforme est en charge du design, de l’implémentation ainsi que de la maintenance des stratégies de trading systématiques pour la base des clients. Utilisant des techniques mathématiques et analytiques avancées, l’équipe développe des solutions adaptées aux opportunités d’investissement, ainsi que pour la couverture et gestion de portefeuille.

La plateforme SGI opère en Europe, en Asie ainsi qu’en Amérique, ou le mandat régional s’inscrit dans un écosystème global.

Quel sera votre quotidien ?

 Support de la production quotidienne du périmètre SGI AMER, qui comprend le calcul précis du niveau d’indices, les rapports automatises des clients ainsi que l’exécution des rebalancements.
 Adresser les différentes demandes et requêtes des traders, ingénieurs et vendeurs au sujet de l’inventaire sur les différentes classes d’actifs.
 Contribuer à l’amélioration continue des procédures SGI dans la perspective d’un set up opérationnel robuste.
 Implémenter des templates standards qui permettent de simplifier la création et maintenance de la création des indices, gérer un cycle de lancement soutenu et assurer une réponse compétitive quant aux délais de traitement.
 Développer et intégrer des métriques quantitatives et des contrôles au sein de l’écosystème SGI pour assurer une bonne gestion des workflows et des dépendances transverses.
 Améliorer et maintenir une base de documents centralisée de la plateforme SGI, les workflows, les contrôles, ainsi que les procédures.
 Engagement avec l’équipe technologie et les partenaires de données externes afin d’ingérer des données volumineuses, développer les procédures d’intégrité de la donnée, ceci dans un objectif de consommation quotidienne des modèles de calcul.
 Participer à l’implémentation d’outils centralises de gestion des risques, donnant des vues dédiées aux équipes d’ingénierie et trading pour améliorer la gestion de l’inventaire SGI.
 Collaborer avec les équipes de trading, d’ingénierie et de la vente pour effectuer les analyses de tendance, de performance, ainsi que de nouvelles solutions et design qui aideront à développer la franchise.
 Apprendre les fondations de la plateforme cross-asset SGI, naviguer les différents systèmes dans une approche de recherche et développement, d’innovation et d’implémentation de nouvelles solutions optimisées.

 Et si c’était vous ?

Compétences techniques :

 Compétences quantitatives et analytiques avancées

 Analytique / Quantitatif / Réactif et adaptatif

ENVIRONNEMENT DE TRAVAIL HYBRIDE:

Société Générale propose un régime de travail hybride qui offre aux employés la possibilité de travailler à distance, ainsi que sur place, afin de promouvoir l'interaction et la collaboration avec les collègues tout en adhérant à tous les protocoles standard de SG. Les modalités de travail hybride varient en fonction du secteur d'activité. Les secteurs d'activité concernés détermineront et communiqueront les modalités de travail qui répondent le mieux à leurs besoins.

Société Générale respecte l’équité en matière d'emploi, et nous sommes fiers de faire de la diversité une force pour notre entreprise. Nous nous engageons à reconnaître et à promouvoir les talents et les réalisations de nos employés et de notre personnel, indépendamment de leur race, de leur religion, de leur couleur de peau, de leur lieu d'origine, de leur sexe, de leur situation de handicap, de leur âge, de leur genre, de leur orientation sexuelle et de toute autre caractéristique ou statut protégé par la législation en vigueur. Nous nous efforçons de rédiger nos affichages de la manière la plus inclusive possible. Si toutefois l'un des deux genres est utilisé seul dans cet affichage, il désigne les personnes de toutes les identités de genre.

About Agoda

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 3.6 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

Get to Know our Team: 

In Product, ideas come alive. The world is moving fast so our culture empowers ownership and minimal bureaucracy. That’s the environment that enables you to do what you think is right – and quickly. Product Operations is a large, multicultural team of diversely talented individuals that serve as the curators of Agoda’s content. We manage all the content our customers and partners see on each of our products. As a part of our team, you will take ownership of processes that are critical to multiple other teams across the business. We are driving property-level content to map inventories from 3 rd  party supplies which will enable our reach to span the globe. Content Operations is also keen on self-improvement and innovation. We run our own structured data and analyze it to make impactful decisions. With the support of state-of-the-art technology and an enriching work environment, we strengthen the bottom line and drive new business for Agoda. 

The Opportunity: 

As an Analyst/Senior Analyst, you will report directly to either the Senior Manager or Associate Director within the Product Department and this will be an individual contributor role. You will be responsible and fully empowered to work with the partners on the ground. You will be supported by a team within the Product department and work closely with other Team members within Agoda. You will be instrumental in ensuring there is consistency in data being used for reporting, identifying value-added data to help the business grow as well as using data to make strategic business decisions. You will be expected to dig into data to provide business insights, guide decision-making and offer valuable inputs to further grow our business model.

In this Role, you’ll get to:

Translate internal briefs into analytical projects (to include refining the initial brief and asking the ‘right questions’, working through potential hypotheses and storyboarding the output)
Use and analyze data from multiple large-scale data warehouses and present statistically strong analysis to a wide range of business stakeholders
Conducted an analysis of customer behavior and their path through the platform, guaranteeing that the conversion rates for each front-end page met the established benchmarks and continually pinpointed opportunities for enhancement
Partnered with the Product Design and User Research team to generate fresh data-driven projects, one of which involved the development of a Dashboard designed for more efficient monitoring of user behavior and the measurement of novel business metrics
Drive new analytical initiatives and projects aimed at improving organizational efficiency and shaping Agoda supply
Identify, support, and lead projects aimed at scaling up the way the Supply organization leverages on data, insights, and intelligence
Automate manual operational processes and present back on time savings gained through modernization of business operations

What you’ll Need to Succeed:

Bachelor’s degree or higher in Mathematics, Business, Economics, Data Science, Information Technology or similar field
Bachelor’s Degree or higher in computer sciences, engineering, mathematics, statistics, data science or a related degree program. Masters degree preferred
Advanced domain of data analysis and data visualization tools and software such as Excel, SQL, Tableau, Python or similar
Analytical mindset, with proven track record in using data to measure performance and make decisions
Excellent problem-solving skills including the ability to analyze and resolve complex problems using data
Ability to work under pressure in a fast-paced and rapidly changing environment
Excellent communication skills (both verbal and written), with proven ability to convey complex messages clearly and with conviction
Team player with strong interpersonal, relationship-building, and stakeholder management skills
