About the job
As the largest operating company in the integrated TransLink enterprise, Coast Mountain Bus Company (CMBC) operates a fleet of clean-fuel conventional and community shuttle buses, zero-emission trolley buses, and passenger ferry SeaBuses in Metro Vancouver, the largest single transit service area in Canada.

At CMBC, one of BC’s Top Employers, we're committed to providing an innovative, healthy, and engaging workforce. This is reflected in our workforce of over 5,500 employees performing over 400 unique jobs, who are committed and empowered to deliver service that attracts nearly 1.1 million passengers daily and connects people, businesses, and communities in the Metro Vancouver region.

We have the important job of helping our passengers get to work, appointments, visiting with family and friends, and back again every day. Metro Vancouver relies on us, and we take that as a point of pride.

Responsibilities
PRIMARY PURPOSE
Represents the Asset Management Team in facilitating technical support and expertise in Enterprise Asset Management (EAM) applications and data analysis as it applies to Infrastructure Maintenance assets.

Work with departments to identify requirements, gather information, propose, and implement new procedures, applications, enhancements, system configuration changes, and liaise with BTS to ensure standards and procedures comply within company policy. 

Coordinates with external support teams to ensure Asset Management and EAM organizational systems are functioning in accordance with business needs and requirements. 

Provides guidance, expertise, and recommendations to various asset management stakeholders in CMBC and TransLink on various reporting systems, analytical tools, processes, and requirements to ensure information availability, quality, integrity, and reliability is maintained. 

Conducts complex analysis, forecasting, reporting and documentation to improve effectiveness and to support continuous improvement of the Enterprise Asset Management systems for the division. 

Provides training to various stakeholders on EAM reporting systems, analytical tools, processes, and requirements. 

Participating in the conceptual workshops and providing technical insights for upgrading and advancement of Enterprise Asset Management Systems directly affecting the betterment of future versions.

ILLUSTRATIVE EXAMPLES OF ACCOUNTABILITY
Provides technical and business guidance to business representatives and subject matter experts regarding the development and implementation of asset management process refinements, including repair versus replace decision models and related requirements for organization’s Infrastructure records and master data updates and corrections (EAM).

Identifies, locates, documents, records, and verifies all CMBC received asset data. Consult on data received from capital projects to confirm the compliance of the CMBC asset attributes and the asset naming convention according to defined asset data acquisition plans, processes, and safety standards.

Evaluating and understanding asset data requirement, conditions, and identification, including data sources, specifications, and safety standards.

Using data acquisition templates and data collection equipment such as handheld mobile devices to collect asset data.

Implementing submittal and transmittal process for asset management drawings and records to ensure all new documents and current versions of records from a closed out and completed projects are received and updated in both EAM and GIS (Geographic Information System) systems.

Documenting asset data into Asset Management tools and software.

Conducting site visits and stakeholder meetings.

Compiling and reviewing records and CAD drawings from various sources.

Ensuring asset data and drawings accurately reflect asset configuration and/or site condition.

Ensuring configuration management is being practiced; and

Supporting in updating and maintaining CAD drawings, maps, reports, and other Asset Management outputs as required.

Maintains asset data and maintenance data, and ensures data accuracy and integrity by:

Reviewing all asset data and CAD drawings received and collected from various resources to ensure data currency and integrity by implementing document control best practices.

Maintaining and updating asset and maintenance data in both Infrastructure EAM and GIS databases by checking information accuracy, currency/version control, and integrity of asset data and CAD drawings are properly reflected.

Conducting site visits and working closely with stakeholders and team members to verify the data currency and accuracy.

Ensuring conformance to Asset Management standards and system design.

Providing support in maintenance of infrastructure asset data including procedures and manuals, work instructions, checklists, failure codes, star charts, etc., by ensuring regular updates to reflect changes and improvements.

Maintaining infrastructure asset data including individual records and attributes, hierarchies, categories, sub-components, condition, bill of materials, etc.; and

Maintaining defined safety information such as hazards, or personal protective equipment required for specific maintenance activities.

Maintaining and analyzing infrastructure asset maintenance drawings and records to develop, revise and maintain Capital Improvement and Maintenance Programs.

Attending to and collaborating with the GIS and EAM Technical group on regular or project meetings to ensure information on jurisdictional and responsibility maps are correctly reflected.

Supports the Asset Management department to develop asset acquisition plans and templates, priorities, and processes by:

Creating asset data acquisition status reports.

Liaising with other departments and external suppliers to determine requirements needed to create, test, and implement operational and statistical reports using various tools and enterprise asset management systems.

Providing expertise in the development, review and improvement of various standards related to infrastructure system assets.

Providing guidance and advice to CMBC enterprise asset management system users to ensure information availability, quality, integrity, and reliability is maintained.

Developing, reviewing, and updating asset management system processes, procedures, documentation, guidelines, and manuals, ensuring accuracy, current, and easily accessible to the Asset management team, to increase retention of processes within Maintenance division.

Providing feedback based on experience gained while utilizing the templates and following the processes.

Providing regular status reports, feedback, and recommendations to the Assistant Manager.

Delivering comprehensive training to student co-ops or other members of the Asset Management team as needed, coupled with regular opportunities for job shadowing.

Qualifications
EDUCATION
The requirements of the job are typically acquired through a post-secondary diploma in a discipline related to Civil, Mechanical or Electrical Engineering, or Computer Science.

EXPERIENCE
Up to three (3) years of hands-on experience in an industrial/utility or transportation environment with diverse and specialized infrastructure assets and systems; including experience coordinating and conducting the identification, cataloguing, geo-locating and maintenance of assets and configurations within a regulated environment; including the time on the job to become familiar with the company’s asset management procedures, standards, and safety requirement. Valid Class 5 BC Driver’s License required.

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking to hire a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Intelligence Analysis Cell (IAC) to focus on eCrime. This position will primarily conduct analysis on established and emerging actors in the eCrime ecosystem, criminal operating models, monetization techniques, and the geographic diversity of eCrime. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into the strategic context and operating environment of adversaries through finished intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders.

What You'll Do

Analyze financially-motivated cyber actors and compose long- and short-form finished intelligence reports related to actor tracking, monetization methods, commodity and closed malware groups, and fraud techniques
Research, assess, and report on specific cyber threat actor and adversary capabilities, motivations, and Tactics, Techniques, and Procedures (TTPs)
Provide clear and concise written responses to customer requests for information (RFIs) and contribute to briefings where necessary
Work in a collaborative environment with other analysts, technical experts, and customer-facing personnel
Assist in research prioritization efforts and intelligence gap identification

What You'll Need

5+ years’ experience conducting research in the field of eCrime to include producing intelligence assessments and handling ad-hoc requests for information (RFIs)
A strong understanding of current and emerging threats related to financially-motivated computer intrusions, scams, and fraud techniques
In-depth knowledge of current underground criminal forums and marketplaces, digital currency use in criminal activity, enabling infrastructures, monetization methods, money laundering, and access brokers
A general understanding of commonly used criminal malware, botnets, and access brokers
An ability to express complex technical and non-technical concepts verbally, graphically, and in writing
Excellent English writing and open-source research skills
Comprehensive practical knowledge of intelligence analysis and collection skills
An analytic mindset capable of applying best practices such as structured analysis, awareness of biases and other pitfalls, and critical thinking in source evaluation
Undergraduate degree in cybersecurity, general intelligence studies, security studies, criminal justice, political science, international relations; or equivalent military training and experience in a cyber intelligence/security MOS
Technical and non-technical security certifications pertaining to financial crimes analysis, anti-money laundering (AML), or cyber threat intelligence

Preferred

Graduate or professional degrees in any of the aforementioned fields
Ability to utilize graph analysis tools (e.g., i2 Analyst Notebook, Maltego) to create both working-level and presentation-grade visualization charts
Experience contributing to Computer Network Operations (CNO) campaign tracking, including working with technical indicators pertaining to malware and network infrastructure
Formal foreign language training or competency, especially in Russian, Farsi, Chinese, Spanish, or Portuguese

About the job
Who are we?

Equinix is the world’s digital infrastructure company®, operating over 250 data centers across the globe. Digital leaders harness Equinix's trusted platform to bring together and interconnect foundational infrastructure at software speed. Equinix enables organizations to access all the right places, partners and possibilities to scale with agility, speed the launch of digital services, deliver world-class experiences and multiply their value, while supporting their sustainability goals.

A career at Equinix means you will collaborate on work that impacts the world and be surrounded by endless opportunities to learn new skills and grow in varied directions. We embrace diversity in thought and contribution and are committed to providing an equitable work environment that is foundational to our core values as a company and is vital to our success. 

Sustainability Analytics Senior Analyst

Equinix is the world’s digital infrastructure company, operating 250 data centers across the globe and providing interconnections to all the key clouds and networks. Businesses need one place to simplify and bring together fragmented, complex infrastructure that spans private and public cloud environments. Our global platform allows customers to place infrastructure wherever they need it and connect it to everything they need to succeed.

We are a fast-growing global company with 20+ years of continuous growth. Through our innovative portfolio of high-performance products and services, we have created the largest, most active global ecosystem of 10,000+ companies, including 2,000+ networks and 3,000+ cloud and IT service providers in 32 countries spanning six continents.

A career at Equinix means you will collaborate on work that impacts the world and be surrounded by endless opportunities to learn new skills and grow in varied directions. We embrace diversity in thought and contribution and are committed to providing an equitable work environment that is foundational to our core values as a company and is vital to our success.

Job Summary

The focus of the role is to lead the development, aggregation, and documentation of business logic and calculation methodologies for sustainability data across the organization. This individual will sit within the Sustainability Program Office (SPO) and will work cross-functionally to develop internal requirements for the sustainability data lake, create data models for managing the corporate GHG inventory, and partner with the product team to define the logic for allocation of environmental data flows (carbon, water, etc) to customers. Candidates will be familiar with agile & sprint project management, ELT (extract, transform, load) pipelines, working in structured and non-structured data bases, as well as have experience with Power BI & Tableau.

Responsibilities

Responsible for developing & documenting business logic and calculation methodologies for sustainability and environmental data 
Cross-functionally collaborate with the product development team to create an organization-wide data lake for sustainability and environmental data 
Own prioritization and pipelines for data configuration & modeling 
Define and document requirements for environmental sustainability dashboard creation 
Drive customer support sustainability data issues to resolution 
Support the creation of feature validation test cases for sustainability products 
Partner with customer-facing teams, the SPO, Business Development, and Marketing to translate future customer sustainability data requirements into product features 
Expectation to grow into an expert on data center, real estate and technology-related sustainability topics including deep expertise in technical sustainability concepts relevant to Equinix’s industry 

Qualifications

1+ years of experience in sustainability 
3+ years of experience in data science, analytics, or product 
2+ years of experience with Power BI & Tableau preferred but not required 
Bachelor’s degree or equivalent in environmental science, statistics, mathematics, accounting, data science, or relevant STEM discipline required 
Master’s or MBA preferred but not required 
Familiar with ETL (extract, transform, load) pipelines and working with both structured and non-structured datasets 
Strong attention to detail and the ability to translate complex sustainability topics to a broad range of audiences 
Working knowledge of sustainability programs specific to energy, environment and emissions (e.g. CDP, GRI, The Greenhouse Gas Protocol, Science-based Targets Initiative, etc.) 
Demonstrated ability to manage multiple work streams with competing and sometimes urgent deadlines and experience influencing upwards to keep programs and projects moving 
Communicate clearly and effectively: verbally, in writing and through presentations; successfully interfacing with internal and external constituents

Equinix is an Equal Employment Opportunity and, in the U.S., an Affirmative Action employer. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to unlawful consideration of race, color, religion, creed, national or ethnic origin, ancestry, place of birth, citizenship, sex, pregnancy / childbirth or related medical conditions, sexual orientation, gender identity or expression, marital or domestic partnership status, age, veteran or military status, physical or mental disability, medical condition, genetic information, political / organizational affiliation, status as a victim or family member of a victim of crime or abuse, or any other status protected by applicable law.

The targeted pay range for this position in the following location is / locations are:

California (Non-SF/Bay Area), Connecticut, Maryland, New York, New Jersey, Washington state: $82,000 to $130,000 per year

We offer flexible work-from-home opportunities for people with passion for languages. The jobs are part-time, and there is no fixed schedule. Whoever you are, wherever you come from, come join our global AI community. www.telusinternational.com

We are hiring freelance English speaking Online Data Analysts for a project aimed at improving the content and quality of digital maps, which are used by millions of users globally. The job would suit someone who is detail-oriented, likes doing research and has a good knowledge of national and local geography. 
 This is a freelance position on a flexible schedule - you can work in your own time whenever work is available. You will be completing research and evaluation tasks in a web-based environment, eg verifying and comparing data, determining the relevance and accuracy of information. You will be provided with guidelines for each task, which need to be followed. The project offers a variety of tasks, and work is paid per task. 

Requirements
Full Professional Proficiency in English
You must be living in Canada for the last 2 consecutive years
Ability to follow guidelines and do research online using search engines, online maps and website information
You must have familiarity with current and historical business, media, sport, news, social media and cultural affairs in Canada 
Being open to work across a diverse set of Task Types (e.g. News, Audio tasks, Relevance)
Applicants must be 18 years or over. 

Working on this project will require you to go through a standard recruitment process (including passing an open book assessment). This is a long-term project and your work will occasionally be subject to quality assurance checks.

Department: Information Technology

YOUR ROLE

The Aldo Group is a leading player based in Montreal in the fashion sector, specializing in shoes and accessories. Known for its trendy designs and its commitment to a high-quality customer experience, Aldo operates under various brands, including ALDO, Call It Spring, and Globo. Beyond its significant in-store presence, Aldo also has a strong digital footprint thanks to its e-commerce. In addition to its leadership in the fashion arena, the Aldo Group is devoted to sustainability, social responsibility, and reducing its ecological footprint.

Responsibilities:

Analyze and understand data needs to provide suitable solutions.
Collaborate closely with various teams to translate business needs into technical specifications.
Ingest, transform, and manage data from a variety of sources.
Deliver high-quality data products: comprehensible, organized, efficient, secure, and documented.
Ensure data security at various levels using tools like AWS Lake Formation and Amazon Quicksight.
Actively participate in the development and improvement of our CI/CD process.

DO YOU HAVE THE PROFILE WE'RE LOOKING FOR?

Required Skills:

Strong proficiency in SQL and data analysis.
Experience with Aldo's data analysis tools ecosystem: AWS Redshift, Amazon S3, DynamoDB, AWS Glue, Amazon Quicksight, and Python.
Ability to translate business needs into technical solutions.
Good communication skills and ability to work in a team.

Assets:

Knowledge of the Retail, Fashion & Wholesale sector.
Experience with ERP systems such as SAP ECC FMS and SAP CAR.
Familiarity with AWS SageMaker and R.
Experience or knowledge in the "Supply Chain Management" sector.

Qualifications:

Degree in computer science, software engineering, or a related field.
A minimum of 3 years of experience as a data analyst and engineer.

Working Conditions:

Possibility of remote work, but must be available to work at the office at least two days per week.
Must operate within the Montreal time zone.

About the job
Reference:

23000UDF

Responsibilities

RISQ’s main mission is to contribute to develop SG Group (the Group) business and returns through the implementation of an efficient risk management process. The VIE will work for a team (RISQ/COO) in charge of Governance, Risk and Compliance (GRC) project, Regulatory projects, and Ad-hoc requests from the Risk Managers.

The VIE will assist with the Governance, Risk Management and Compliance (GRC) initiative and his/her mission will be focused around 4 areas:

 Data analysis and identification of trends and data improvements
 Data quality checks to identify data quality issues
 Find opportunities to use Machine Learning / Artificial Intelligence and build the proof of concept
 Data reporting through BI Tool such as PowerBI

The GRC initiative aims to harmonize and integrate all risks and controls processes across multiple departments (RISQ, IT Risk, Compliance, Finance, Legal, etc.). The GRC tool developed for the initiative is named RSA Archer and currently has 150+ modules used mainly in the America region. Occasionally, the VIE will also support Risk Managers on ad-hoc requests.

Data analysis

 Analyze Archer data to ensure consistency of referential data uses (i.e.: organizational, geography, legal entity) and feasibility of reporting requirements
 Escalate any data issues such as duplication of records, unreportable multi selects, invalid records, etc.
 Review impact analysis on referential or taxonomy changes
 Perform ad hoc checks to guarantee data integrity
 Clean and normalize the data

Data quality

 Gather data quality needs with various risk teams
 Develop automatic checks on data
 Perform regular and automatized checks to ensure that data quality in GRC tool is good. Checks will include completeness of information as well as simple data quality checks (i.e.: events reported within # days)

ML/AI

 Identify opportunity for Machine Learning / Artificial Intelligence
 Gather Business Requirements and needs from end users
 Develop Proof of Concept and perform demo to end users

Reporting support

 Develop reports/dashboards in BI tool (Power BI) as per reporting needs provided

Provide demo to end users and release to production environment

Required

 Profile required

PLEASE NOTE that since this program is primarily an international development program, candidates cannot apply for a VIE assignment in their own country of citizenship.

To facilitate the examination of your application by our English-speaking managers, we thank you for applying in English.

Studies & experience:

 Graduate with a Master degree from Business/Engineering School or University; a specialization in Engineering and/or Computer Science will be a plus
 A previous experience in Business Intelligence Tool such as Microsoft Power BI or Tableau would be appreciated

Language skills:

 Fluent in English (B2-C1)

Technical, operational & Soft skills:

 Proficient/Good command of MS Office
 Good communication and presentation skills
 Python or knowledge of another language (VBA/Java/C#/JavaScript); willingness to learn Python (must have)
 Data analysis skills, database, and SQL (must have)
 Time management & organizational skills to be able to do manage multiple bulk of work simultaneously (must have)
 Experience in reporting and data aggregation (will be a plus)
 Experience in Machine Learning / Artificial Intelligence (will be a plus)
 Knowledge of risk management and/or GRC tool (will be extremely valued)
 BA skills to translate Business needs in requirements (will be a plus)

The VIE assignment in a nutshell

This VIE in Montreal is to begin as soon as possible but you need to plan 3 months between your application date and the beginning of your VIE assignment. It will last 24 months.

In case a visa is necessary, please make sure your passport is valid up to 6 months after the end of the VIE contract to not delay your departure.

The VIE is a specific contract, under Business France’s eligibility criteria, opened to candidates under 28 and from the member states of the European Economic Space. For further information (including your financial indemnities), please see Mon VIE-VIA Business France.

We would like to draw your attention to the fact there that your VIE mission could potentially get postponed, depending on the evolution of the health crisis and subjects to the decision made by the Crisis and Support Centre of the Ministry of Europe and Foreign Affairs (MEAE). In addition, the selected candidate will only be paid upon confirmation from Business France and arrival in the country of assignment.

 Why join us

As soon as you arrive, you will be integrated into our teams and will learn every day alongside our experts, who will support you in your tasks. Gradually, you will become more independent in your projects, making this experience a real career accelerator. You will also discover all the diversity of our businesses, in a sector that is constantly evolving and innovating.

At the end of your V.I.E. contract, various opportunities could be offered to you, in Canada and abroad.

 Business insight

At Société Générale, we are convinced that people are drivers of change, and that the world of tomorrow will be shaped by all their initiatives, from the smallest to the most ambitious.

Whether you’re joining us for a period of months, years or your entire career, together we can have a positive impact on the future. Creating, daring, innovating and taking action are part of our DNA.

If you too want to be directly involved, grow in a stimulating and caring environment, feel useful on a daily basis and develop or strengthen your expertise, you will feel right at home with us!

Still hesitating?

You should know that our employees can dedicate several days per year to solidarity actions during their working hours, including sponsoring people struggling with their orientation or professional integration, participating in the financial education of young apprentices, and sharing their skills with charities. There are many ways to get involved.

Societe Generale is an equal opportunity employer, and we are proud to make diversity a strength for our company. We are committed to recognizing and promoting the talents and achievements of our employees and staff, regardless of race, religion, color, national origin, sex, disability, age, gender, sexual orientation, and any other characteristic or status protected under applicable law. We strive to write our postings as inclusively as possible. If, however, one of the two genders is used alone in this display, it designates persons of all gender identities.
About the job
Inspirantes, ingénieuses, animées de l’esprit d’entreprise : voilà ce qui décrit bien nos équipes d’exception. Donnez une vocation à votre passion en rejoignant une culture qui s’épanouit face au changement.

Faites votre marque au sein du Groupe des normes professionnelles en certification - Conception des méthodes de certification à titre de directeur(trice). Cette équipe diversifiée de professionnels mise sur son expertise technique et sectorielle pour contribuer, à l’interne, au succès de notre pratique de certification et de comptabilité. En tant que conseiller de confiance, vous jouerez un rôle influent en matière de nouvelles tendances et de changements pour vous assurer que nos membres répondent aux normes les plus rigoureuses du secteur.

Notre identité canadienne est pour nous une source de fierté. Nous sommes un cabinet de comptabilité, de fiscalité et de services-conseils de premier plan au Canada qui propose des stratégies et des solutions aux entreprises. Entrepreneurs dans l’âme, les membres talentueux de notre équipe voient les obstacles comme des occasions de se dépasser et transforment les façons de faire sur le marché des petites et moyennes entreprises.

Responsabilités

Promouvoir l’importance du contrôle de la qualité auprès des associés, des directeurs et des autres membres du cabinet et jouer un rôle central dans les initiatives du cabinet visant la qualité.
Appuyer la conception et la mise à jour des politiques et des lignes directrices encadrant les missions du cabinet de même que ses protocoles de comptabilité et d’audit.
Se tenir au courant des changements dans la profession en effectuant des recherches et en prenant part à des activités et à des séances de formation organisées dans le secteur.
Contribuer à la conception et faciliter la mise en œuvre des formations en certification dans le cadre des programmes de perfectionnement interne exhaustifs de MNP.
Entretenir des liens et des échanges professionnels avec les équipes de certification et de comptabilité du cabinet et avec ses équipes de direction.
Acquérir une solide compréhension des services de MNP ainsi que des entreprises et des secteurs servis par le cabinet.
Prendre part à l’élaboration de nouvelles idées et méthodes pour améliorer les procédures de travail.
Optimiser les effectifs afin qu’un travail complet et exact soit livré dans le respect des échéances.
Fournir un mentorat aux membres de l’équipe, les motiver et les encadrer pour qu’ils puissent se perfectionner et s’épanouir grâce à des objectifs clairs, à une rétroaction régulière et à une résolution rapide des problèmes de rendement, en plus de procéder aux évaluations de rendement.
Être disposé à se déplacer, au besoin.


Compétences et expérience 

Minimum de deux ans d'expérience à titre de comptable principal(e) dans le service de certification d’un des sept grands cabinets comptables et expérience antérieure en certification
Expérience de la conception et la mise en œuvre de procédures d’audit fondées sur le risque et le caractère significatif
Capacité de communiquer et d'écrire en Français et en anglais 
Connaissance des
Contrôles internes et de leur application
Diverses normes comptables (p. ex., NCECF, NCOSBL, NCSP)
Interprétation et application des normes de certification (p. ex., NCA et/ou ISA)
Compétences en rédaction technique et en gestion de projets; compréhension des principes commerciaux, de gestion et d’expansion des affaires s’appliquant à un cabinet

MesAvantages@MNP 

Offrant un potentiel de revenus élevés, MNP est fier de proposer des avantages taillés sur mesure qui sont à l’image de notre culture d’exception et qui favorisent un mode de vie équilibré, le tout pour aider ses membres à s’épanouir, tant au bureau que dans leur vie personnelle. Vous profiterez d’un salaire de base généreux, de vacances, de quatre congés personnels payés par année, d’un régime collectif de retraite avec cotisations égalées à 4 %, de produits d’épargne volontaire, de programmes de primes, d’avantages sociaux à la carte, de ressources en santé mentale, d’un accès exclusif à des rabais et à des avantages indirects, d’une aide au perfectionnement professionnel, de cours offerts à l’interne par l’intermédiaire de MNP University, d’un code vestimentaire adapté à vos tâches, d’activités sociales organisées par le cabinet, et plus encore!

Diversité@MNP

Chez MNP, la diversité est l’une de nos valeurs de base et nous célébrons nos différences. Nous croyons que chaque membre de notre cabinet apporte ses talents uniques et que la mise en valeur de son potentiel nous rend collectivement plus forts. Nous encourageons les personnes vivant avec un handicap à poser leur candidature.

Capacité de communiquer et d'écrire en Français et en anglais 
Connaissance des
Contrôles internes et de leur application

Compétences en rédaction technique et en gestion de projets; compréhension des principes commerciaux, de gestion et d’expansion des affaires s’appliquant à un cabinet

About the job
About Agoda

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 3.6 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

THIS ROLE IS BASED IN BANGKOK, THAILAND (WITH RELOCATION PROVIDED)

Location: Bangkok, Thailand (*Not open for remote work.)

Get to Know our Team:

As part of the Supply Analytics, you will be responsible for identifying new partners and opportunities, cultivating a relationship with them, and working together with them to deliver the best outcome for our end customers. You would also be responsible with managing the day-to-day interaction with the partner and working closely with other teams within Agoda to ensure the partners needs are met.

We design tailored business and product solutions with our partners and help them generate measurable value. Members of our team are empowered and supported to grow their market(s) or accounts. We develop win-win relationships and leverage Agoda’s unique accommodations portfolio and tech solutions to bring our partners the advantages they seek. Utilizing our strong brand and resources, we build new channels to increase the visibility of Agoda, introduce more travelers to our great products and service and deliver significant revenues to the overall business.

The Opportunity: 

As an Analyst/Senior Analyst, you will report directly to either the Senior Manager or Associate Director within the Supply Department and this will be an individual contributor role. You will be responsible and fully empowered to work with the partners on the ground. You will be supported by a team within the Supply department and work closely with other Team members within Agoda.

In this Role, you’ll get to:

Translate internal briefs into analytical projects (to include refining the initial brief and asking the ‘right questions’, working through potential hypotheses and storyboarding the output)
Use and analyze data from multiple large-scale data warehouses and present statistically strong analysis to a wide range of business stakeholders
Proactively identify opportunities for growth within supply and the wider business
Drive new analytical initiatives and projects aimed at improving organizational efficiency and shaping Agoda supply
Identify, support, and lead projects aimed at scaling up the way the Supply organization leverages on data, insights, and intelligence
Automate manual operational processes and present back on time savings gained through modernization of business operations

What you’ll Need to Succeed:

At least 3-5+ years of experience working as an Analyst with experience in analytics/data science/insights/strategy/BI
Advanced working knowledge and hands-on experience in SQL
Strong knowledge and hands-on experience in data visualization tools such as Tableau (preferably) 
Expert domain of data analysis and data visualization tools and software such as Excel, Python (or R)
Bachelor’s degree ideally in a business or quantitative subject (e.g. computer science, mathematics, engineering, science, economics or finance)
A good understanding of statistical modelling knowledge or any machine learning technique knowledge (such as hypothesis testing, regression, logistic regression, random forest, etc.)
Good stakeholder management experience. Comfortable presenting to senior leadership and C-suite
Experience in conducting A/B testing experimentation
Strong experience in finding data insights and provide business recommendation to the business
A hacker’s mindset – the ability to build simple but clever and elegant solutions to new problems within significant resource, operational and time constraints through deep understanding of the business, creative problem solving, and a wide range of expertise in data, analytics, automation, programming, and prototyping
Excellent communicator with superior written, verbal, presentation and interpersonal communication skills
Data driven in both decision making and performance measurement
Extreme comfort in ambiguous, fast-paced environment
Ability to multi-task, prioritize and coordinate resources

It’s Great if you Have: 

MBA or Masters in a quantitative subject (e.g. computer science, mathematics, engineering, science, economics or finance)
Program management certifications (e.g. PMI, PRINCE2) to compliment your program management experience
Asian market experience
Travel industry / e-commerce / tech / consulting experience

Renseignements généraux

Vous avez envie d’action ? De travailler au sein d’une équipe dynamique ? De participer à l’amélioration de la qualité de vie des Québécoises et des Québécois ? Saisissez cette occasion de mettre de l’avant votre implication et votre créativité afin de faire concrètement la différence. Le ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable (le Ministère) vous offre notamment un milieu de vie qui privilégie de nouvelles pratiques de gestion audacieuses et mieux adaptées aux réalités de la nouvelle génération. Grâce à l’approche Entreprise en santé, le Ministère est soucieux de la qualité de vie au travail de son personnel et désire offrir un milieu collaboratif, mobilisateur et respectueux, qui favorise la santé et le mieux-être des personnes. Laissez-vous transporter vers de nouveaux défis et joignez-vous au ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable !

Vous êtes à la recherche d’une opportunité exceptionnelle pour développer votre carrière et vous aimeriez contribuer à l’essor de l’intelligence artificielle dans le domaine des transports ? Rejoignez-nous aujourd’hui et faites partie d’une équipe passionnée qui écrira une nouvelle page de l’ère numérique!

 Analyste des données 

 Direction générale : Direction générale des ressources informationnelles et de la transformation numérique (DGRITN) 
 Direction générale adjointe : Direction générale adjointe de la gouvernance, de la sécurité informationnelle et de l’intelligence artificielle 
 Direction : Direction de la gouvernance des données et de l’intelligence artificielle (DGDIA) 
 Nombre d’emplois à pourvoir : 1 
 Statut de l’emploi : Régulier 
 Lieu de travail : 900 boulevard René-Lévesque Est, Québec* 
 Télétravail : en mode hybride 
 Horaire de travail : 35 heures par semaine 
 Date prévue d’entrée en fonction : Février 2024 
Étant un ministère qui œuvre partout sur le territoire et considérant la situation actuelle, nous avons l’opportunité de pourvoir cet emploi dans n’importe quelle région où il se trouve un bureau du ministère des Transports et la Mobilité durable

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci. 

 Les avantages de travailler au ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable 

 Régime de retraite à prestations déterminées avantageux ; 
 Régime d’assurances collectives ; 
 20 jours de vacances après seulement un an de service et 13 jours fériés ; 
 Mesures de conciliation travail et vie personnelle ; 
 Horaire variable ; 
 Sécurité d’emploi ; 
 Programme d’aide aux employés (PAE) ; 
 Programme de soutien aux études ; 
 Service de formation et de développement au sein de l’organisation ; 
 Soutien financier à la pratique d’activités physiques. 

 Salaire annuel : 

51 776 $ à 90 110 $ selon l’expérience

L’échelle salariale peut être consultée sur le site Web du Secrétariat du Conseil du trésor . À l’embauche, l’échelon sera déterminé en fonction de l’expérience du candidat.

La rémunération est déterminée en fonction de la pertinence de votre scolarité et de vos expériences en lien avec l’emploi. Par conséquent, il est important de bien les détailler dans votre formulaire d’inscription qui servira de référence.

Profil recherché

 Les qualités que nous recherchons : 

 S’adapter facilement aux changements et aimer le travail en équipe ; 
 Faire preuve d’autonomie, de créativité et d’initiative ; 
 Démontrer un excellent sens de l’organisation et une grande rigueur ; 
 Posséder une excellente connaissance de la langue française parlée et écrite. 

 La personne recherchée doit satisfaire aux exigences de l’emploi : 

 Détenir un diplôme universitaire de premier cycle dans le domaine de l’informatique, de l’administration ou dans un domaine jugé pertinent dont l’obtention requiert un minimum de 90 crédits ou une attestation d’études pertinentes dont l’équivalence est reconnue par l’autorité compétente. 1 

La candidature d’une personne qui est en voie de terminer la dernière année de scolarité exigée pour l’obtention du diplôme requis pourrait être considérée.

Chaque année de scolarité manquante peut être compensée par une année de scolarité pertinente de niveau égal ou supérieur à celle exigée. Le diplôme exigé peut également être compensé par une maîtrise dans une discipline pertinente comportant un minimum de 45 crédits.

 Posséder au moins une (1) année d’expérience comme analyste des données. 
 Avoir une connaissance du français appropriée aux fonctions ; 
 Posséder la citoyenneté canadienne, le statut de résident permanent ou un permis de travail émis par l’autorité fédérale compétente pour occuper un emploi dans la fonction publique du Québec². 

 Autres éléments du profil recherché : 

 Connaitre l’environnement informationnel et l’intelligence d’affaires en soutien aux besoins stratégiques, tactiques et opérationnels ; 
 Connaitre les outils d’analyse et d’exploitation des données pour des fins de production d’information, notamment : SQL de Oracle, Oracle PL/SQL, PostegreSQL, Microsoft PowerPivot, Power BI, Oracle Discoverer, Python/R et SSRS ; 

Ce ou ces postes sont à pourvoir dans la ou les villes suivantes : Toutes les régions du Québec

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

About Agoda 

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 2.5 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

Get to Know our Team:

Agoda first started selling air tickets in late 2019; we are currently looking to grow the commercial team in North Asia to help grow our young Flights business into a market leader in APAC.

As part of the Flights Team, you will be responsible for identifying new partners and opportunities, cultivating a relationship with them, and working together with them to deliver the best outcome for our end customers. You would also be responsible with managing the day to day interaction with the partner and working closely with other teams within Agoda to ensure the partners needs are met.

The Opportunity:

You will be responsible and fully empowered to work with the partners on the ground. You will be supported by a team within the Supply department and work closely with other Flight Commercial Team members within Agoda.

You will have the opportunity to be part of an exciting and brand new team and new business vertical for Agoda and have the rare opportunity of joining a ‘start-up’ within an established company.

In this Role, you’ll get to:

Translate internal briefs into analytical projects (to include refining the initial brief and asking the ‘right questions’, working through potential hypotheses and storyboarding the output)
Use and analyze data from multiple large-scale data warehouses and present statistically strong analysis to a wide range of business stakeholders
Proactively identify opportunities for growth within supply and the wider business

Identify, support, and lead projects aimed at scaling up the way the Supply organization leverages on data, insights, and intelligence
Automate manual operational processes and present back on time savings gained through modernization of business operations

What you’ll Need to Succeed:

At least 3-5+ years of experience working as an Analyst with experience in analytics/data science/insights/strategy/BI
Advanced working knowledge and hands-on experience in SQL
Strong knowledge and hands-on experience in data visualization tools such as Tableau (preferably) 
Expert domain of data analysis and data visualization tools and software such as Excel, Python (or R)
Bachelor’s degree ideally in a business or quantitative subject (e.g. computer science, mathematics, engineering, science, economics or finance)
A good understanding of statistical modelling knowledge or any machine learning technique knowledge (such as hypothesis testing, regression, logistic regression, random forest, etc.)
Good stakeholder management experience. Comfortable presenting to senior leadership and C-suite
Experience in conducting A/B testing experimentation
Strong experience in finding data insights and provide business recommendation to the business

Excellent communicator with superior written, verbal, presentation and interpersonal communication skills
Data driven in both decision making and performance measurement
Extreme comfort in ambiguous, fast-paced environment
Ability to multi-task, prioritize and coordinate resources

About the job
240001YT

 Vos missions au quotidien

À PROPOS DU POSTE :

Au sein de la Banque d’Affaires et d’Investissement de la Société Générale, la division Marchés Globaux regroupe la recherche, les solutions d’investissement et de gestion des risques, la négociation et règlement de transactions, les services de garde de valeur, pour les actions, obligations, contrats à terme, devises, commodités ainsi que capacités de structurations dans le but de fournir aux investisseurs une plate-forme globale à multiple classes d’actif. Notre activité repose non seulement sur une approche consultative axée sur l’innovation, mais également centrée sur les besoins des clients. La division des Marchés Globaux est un acteur majeur dans les produits dérivés listés et de gré-à-gré mais aussi à travers les différentes classes d’actif ainsi qu’en macro-économie. Notre offre de service en compensation et garde de valeur offre une combinaison unique en ce qui a trait au transactionnel des marchés, compensation des produits dérivés, gardien de valeur et services de financement.

Société Générale Index (SGI) platforme est en charge du design, de l’implémentation ainsi que de la maintenance des stratégies de trading systématiques pour la base des clients. Utilisant des techniques mathématiques et analytiques avancées, l’équipe développe des solutions adaptées aux opportunités d’investissement, ainsi que pour la couverture et gestion de portefeuille.

La plateforme SGI opère en Europe, en Asie ainsi qu’en Amérique, ou le mandat régional s’inscrit dans un écosystème global.

Quel sera votre quotidien ?

 Support de la production quotidienne du périmètre SGI AMER, qui comprend le calcul précis du niveau d’indices, les rapports automatises des clients ainsi que l’exécution des rebalancements.
 Adresser les différentes demandes et requêtes des traders, ingénieurs et vendeurs au sujet de l’inventaire sur les différentes classes d’actifs.
 Contribuer à l’amélioration continue des procédures SGI dans la perspective d’un set up opérationnel robuste.
 Implémenter des templates standards qui permettent de simplifier la création et maintenance de la création des indices, gérer un cycle de lancement soutenu et assurer une réponse compétitive quant aux délais de traitement.
 Développer et intégrer des métriques quantitatives et des contrôles au sein de l’écosystème SGI pour assurer une bonne gestion des workflows et des dépendances transverses.
 Améliorer et maintenir une base de documents centralisée de la plateforme SGI, les workflows, les contrôles, ainsi que les procédures.
 Engagement avec l’équipe technologie et les partenaires de données externes afin d’ingérer des données volumineuses, développer les procédures d’intégrité de la donnée, ceci dans un objectif de consommation quotidienne des modèles de calcul.
 Participer à l’implémentation d’outils centralises de gestion des risques, donnant des vues dédiées aux équipes d’ingénierie et trading pour améliorer la gestion de l’inventaire SGI.
 Collaborer avec les équipes de trading, d’ingénierie et de la vente pour effectuer les analyses de tendance, de performance, ainsi que de nouvelles solutions et design qui aideront à développer la franchise.
 Apprendre les fondations de la plateforme cross-asset SGI, naviguer les différents systèmes dans une approche de recherche et développement, d’innovation et d’implémentation de nouvelles solutions optimisées.

 Et si c’était vous ?

Compétences et qualifications :

Compétences techniques :

 Compétences quantitatives et analytiques avancées
 Habileté en programmation utilisant un langage orienté objet
 Maîtrise des mathématiques appliquées et de la modélisation
 Pratique de l'analyse quantitative avec la capacité de rechercher des problèmes et de les accompagner à travers des solutions établies

Compétences et qualifications :

 Solides compétences en communication et capacité à interagir avec des partenaires clés
 Bonnes compétences organisationnelles et en gestion de projet
 De préférence avec une expérience en stratégies de trading systématiques
 Motivé et capable de travailler en équipe ou seul si nécessaire
 À l'aise avec la complexité organisationnelle, les environnements à haute pression et les changements rapides
 Analytique / Quantitatif / Réactif et adaptatif
 Des compétences en science des données, en statistiques et en analyse de séries temporelles sont souhaitées

Expérience requise :

 3 ans d'expérience dans un poste similaire ou en analyse quantitative
 Forte expérience dans l'utilisation d'un environnement analytique

Éducation :

 Exigence minimale : maitrise en finance et mathématiques

Compétences linguistiques:

L'habilité de communiquer en anglais, tant à l'oral que par écrit, est une exigence puisque la personne occupant ce poste devra collaborer régulièrement avec des collègues et des partenaires situés aux États-Unis.

En raison de l"application de la loi fédérale américaine sur les valeurs mobilières à ce poste, les candidats qui postuleront à ce poste devront se soumettre à une vérification approfondie de leurs antécédents, y compris la collecte de leurs empreintes digitales par un fournisseur tiers sélectionné par la Financial Industry Regulatory Authority («FINRA»)

 Plus qu’un poste, un tremplin

ENVIRONNEMENT DE TRAVAIL HYBRIDE:

Les modalités de travail hybride varient en fonction du secteur d'activité. Les secteurs d'activité concernés détermineront et communiqueront les modalités de travail qui répondent le mieux à leurs besoins.

Société Générale respecte l’équité en matière d'emploi, et nous sommes fiers de faire de la diversité une force pour notre entreprise. Nous nous engageons à reconnaître et à promouvoir les talents et les réalisations de nos employés et de notre personnel, indépendamment de leur race, de leur religion, de leur couleur de peau, de leur lieu d'origine, de leur sexe, de leur situation de handicap, de leur âge, de leur genre, de leur orientation sexuelle et de toute autre caractéristique ou statut protégé par la législation en vigueur. Nous nous efforçons de rédiger nos affichages de la manière la plus inclusive possible. Si toutefois l'un des deux genres est utilisé seul dans cet affichage, il désigne les personnes de toutes les identités de genre.

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking to hire a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Intelligence Analysis Cell (IAC) to focus on eCrime. This position will primarily conduct analysis on established and emerging actors in the eCrime ecosystem, criminal operating models, monetization techniques, and the geographic diversity of eCrime. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into the strategic context and operating environment of adversaries through finished intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders. Particular to this role, CrowdStrike is seeking individuals with knowledge and experience related to cryptocurrency investigations, blockchain analysis, and criminal interactions with illicit and legitimate financial service providers.

What You'll Do

Analyze financially-motivated cyber actors and compose long- and short-form finished intelligence reports related to actor tracking, monetization methods, commodity and closed malware groups, and fraud techniques
Research, assess, and report on specific cyber threat actor and adversary capabilities, motivations, and Tactics, Techniques, and Procedures (TTPs)
Provide clear and concise written responses to customer requests for information (RFIs) and contribute to briefings where necessary
Work in a collaborative environment with other analysts, technical experts, and customer-facing personnel
Assist in research prioritization efforts and intelligence gap identification

Required

What You'll Need:

5+ years’ experience conducting research in the field of eCrime to include producing intelligence assessments and handling ad-hoc requests for information (RFIs)
A strong understanding of current and emerging threats related to financially-motivated computer intrusions, scams, and fraud techniques
In-depth knowledge of current underground criminal forums and marketplaces, digital currency use in criminal activity, enabling infrastructures, monetization methods, money laundering, and access brokers
A general understanding of commonly used criminal malware, botnets, and access brokers
An ability to express complex technical and non-technical concepts verbally, graphically, and in writing
Excellent English writing and open-source research skills
Comprehensive practical knowledge of intelligence analysis and collection skills
An analytic mindset capable of applying best practices such as structured analysis, awareness of biases and other pitfalls, and critical thinking in source evaluation
Undergraduate degree in cybersecurity, general intelligence studies, security studies, criminal justice, political science, international relations; or equivalent military training and experience in a cyber intelligence/security MOS
Technical and non-technical security certifications pertaining to financial crimes analysis, anti-money laundering (AML), or cyber threat intelligence
Technical security certifications pertaining to cryptocurrency investigations or blockchain analysis (e.g., Chainalysis Cryptocurrency Fundamentals Certification [CCFC], Chainalysis Reactor Certification [CRC], TRM Certified Investigator [CI], Elliptic Product Certification, Ciphertrace Blockchain and Cryptocurrency Essentials Certification [BCEC], McAfee Certified Cryptocurrency Forensic Investigator [CCFI], Blockchain Intelligence Group Certified Cryptocurrency Investigator [CCI])

Preferred

Graduate or professional degrees in any of the aforementioned fields
Ability to utilize graph analysis tools (e.g., i2 Analyst Notebook, Maltego) to create both working-level and presentation-grade visualization charts
Experience contributing to Computer Network Operations (CNO) campaign tracking, including working with technical indicators pertaining to malware and network infrastructure
Extensive experience in conducting cryptocurrency investigations pertaining to criminal activity, including analyzing blockchain transaction data and assessing interactions between threat actors and illicit and legitimate financial service providers (e.g., darknet markets, ransomware actors, DeFi platforms, mining pools, mixers, merchant services)
Advanced technical security certifications pertaining to cryptocurrency investigations or blockchain analysis (e.g., Chainalysis Investigation Specialist Certification [CISC], TRM Advanced Crypto Investigator [ACI], Elliptic Specialist Investigator Certification, Ciphertrace Cryptocurrency Tracing Certified Examiner [CTCE])
Formal foreign language training or competency, especially in Russian, Farsi, Chinese, Spanish, or Portuguese

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Global Threat Analysis Cell (GTAC) to focus on targeted intrusion activity related to China-nexus adversaries. This position will be primarily focused on tracking known adversaries and other cyber operations believed to emanate from China, as well as identifying and tracking trends associated with these operations. The Senior Intelligence Analyst will be required to research and report on cyber operations at both the strategic and tactical level as part of a close-knit team where collaboration is a critical driver for mission success. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into adversary operations through finished Intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders.

What You'll Do

Proactively identify and track targeted intrusion cyber threats, trends, and new developments by China-nexus adversaries through analysis of raw intelligence and data 
Apply analytic best practices and tradecraft to gathered intelligence in a consistent manner
Provide finished intelligence analysis and assessments to internal and external customers through written reporting, in varying predetermined suspense and depth, with minimal supervision
Collaborate across teams to inform various functions within CrowdStrike Intelligence about activity of interest and to coordinate adversary/campaign tracking, as well as enrich finished intelligence products
Identify intelligence gaps and submit requests for information to fill gaps
Provide peer review of proposed/draft reporting and analytic uplift to team members 
Prioritize, categorize, and respond to requests for information from internal and external customers
Conduct briefings as needed for a variety of levels of customers as requested (via either phone, video conference, webcast, in-person briefing, or industry conference)

What You'll Need

Motivated self-starter with 5+ years’ experience in a threat intelligence and cybersecurity environment, with a focus on state-nexus cyber operations
Comprehensive, practical knowledge of research/collection tradecraft and analytical methods—to include intrusion analysis
Strong analytic writing skills, particularly the ability to produce quality finished intelligence products on short deadlines as well as continuing to maintain analysis for, and report on, long-term strategic assessments with minimal assistance
Familiarity with computer networking fundamentals, computer network defense (CND) operations, host-based forensics and network traffic monitoring
Ability to independently identify and track adversary tradecraft trends 
Understanding of technical terminology, tools, and tactics employed by threat actors
An enthusiasm for collaboration, including being comfortable working in a team-oriented environment as well as across multiple teams to leverage subject matter expertise of colleagues
Passionate about taking the initiative to identify and develop new visibility into adversary operations
Ability or willingness to learn to conduct technical analysis of the tools and tradecraft used by threat actors
Knowledge of geopolitical issues and ability to use that information to support understanding of current and future impacts on the cyber threat landscape
Undergraduate degree, military training or relevant experience in cyber intelligence, computer science, general intelligence studies, security studies, political science, international relations, etc. 
Other technical security certifications or academic background, such as a graduate degree, are a plus.

Remote-first culture

About the job
Be part of a dynamic team whose primary objective is to add value, optimize our tools and conduct advanced analyses whose findings have a tangible impact on how our business is managed.

The Business Intelligence Analyst is a full-time role within our Project Management Office team. The successful candidate’s primary responsibilities will be to design, produce and distribute a variety of reports, dashboards and performance indicators that will contribute to strategic decision-making.

You’ll Have The Opportunity To

Gathering and compiling business needs; 
Defining the organization’s performance indicators;
Examining and analyzing data;
Designing and updating performance tracking dashboards and reports;
Issuing recommendations to support executives in their decision-making;
Enhancing and refining reports and dashboards on an ongoing basis.

YOU’LL THRIVE IN THIS ROLE IF YOU HAVE THE FOLLOWING SKILLS AND QUALITIES:

Undergraduate degree in organizational information systems, business intelligence, statistics, computer science or equivalent;
Three to five years’ experience in a data analyst or similar role;
Demonstrated leadership and communication skills;
Ability to influence management teams;

About the job
Overview

The Commerce Systems team within Hexagon's Autonomy & Positioning division is looking for a Business & Data Analyst to join our high-tech engineering and manufacturing company that is committed to customer service excellence and continuous improvement. This is a fantastic opportunity to join a dynamic, fast-paced, highly collaborative team in driving tangible and measurable results. Reporting to Team Lead of Business & Data Analysis in the Commerce Systems team, you will interact with key business teams (primarily sales and marketing) while supporting, improving, and extending our commerce system capabilities across our autonomy and positioning portfolio.

The Location: Hexagon is a global company with locations around the world. This position is based onsite in Calgary, AB and we offer hybrid work once both training and onboarding are completed.

Responsibilities

As a Business & Data Analyst, responsibilities include:

 Business Analysis – Take on a BA role on feature definition by:
 Working with stakeholders to clarify business requirements, 
 Facilitate meetings and provide presentations to share ideas and findings 
 Translate stakeholder requirements into system requirements.

About the job

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking to hire a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Intelligence Analysis Cell (IAC) to focus on eCrime. This position will primarily conduct analysis on established and emerging actors in the eCrime ecosystem, criminal operating models, monetization techniques, and the geographic diversity of eCrime. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into the strategic context and operating environment of adversaries through finished intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders. Particular to this role, CrowdStrike is seeking individuals with knowledge and experience related to cryptocurrency investigations, blockchain analysis, and criminal interactions with illicit and legitimate financial service providers.

What You'll Do

Analyze financially-motivated cyber actors and compose long- and short-form finished intelligence reports related to actor tracking, monetization methods, commodity and closed malware groups, and fraud techniques
Research, assess, and report on specific cyber threat actor and adversary capabilities, motivations, and Tactics, Techniques, and Procedures (TTPs)
Provide clear and concise written responses to customer requests for information (RFIs) and contribute to briefings where necessary
Work in a collaborative environment with other analysts, technical experts, and customer-facing personnel
Assist in research prioritization efforts and intelligence gap identification

Required

What You'll Need:

5+ years’ experience conducting research in the field of eCrime to include producing intelligence assessments and handling ad-hoc requests for information (RFIs)
A strong understanding of current and emerging threats related to financially-motivated computer intrusions, scams, and fraud techniques
In-depth knowledge of current underground criminal forums and marketplaces, digital currency use in criminal activity, enabling infrastructures, monetization methods, money laundering, and access brokers
A general understanding of commonly used criminal malware, botnets, and access brokers
An ability to express complex technical and non-technical concepts verbally, graphically, and in writing
Excellent English writing and open-source research skills
Comprehensive practical knowledge of intelligence analysis and collection skills
An analytic mindset capable of applying best practices such as structured analysis, awareness of biases and other pitfalls, and critical thinking in source evaluation
Undergraduate degree in cybersecurity, general intelligence studies, security studies, criminal justice, political science, international relations; or equivalent military training and experience in a cyber intelligence/security MOS
Technical and non-technical security certifications pertaining to financial crimes analysis, anti-money laundering (AML), or cyber threat intelligence
Technical security certifications pertaining to cryptocurrency investigations or blockchain analysis (e.g., Chainalysis Cryptocurrency Fundamentals Certification [CCFC], Chainalysis Reactor Certification [CRC], TRM Certified Investigator [CI], Elliptic Product Certification, Ciphertrace Blockchain and Cryptocurrency Essentials Certification [BCEC], McAfee Certified Cryptocurrency Forensic Investigator [CCFI], Blockchain Intelligence Group Certified Cryptocurrency Investigator [CCI])

Preferred

Graduate or professional degrees in any of the aforementioned fields
Ability to utilize graph analysis tools (e.g., i2 Analyst Notebook, Maltego) to create both working-level and presentation-grade visualization charts
Experience contributing to Computer Network Operations (CNO) campaign tracking, including working with technical indicators pertaining to malware and network infrastructure
Extensive experience in conducting cryptocurrency investigations pertaining to criminal activity, including analyzing blockchain transaction data and assessing interactions between threat actors and illicit and legitimate financial service providers (e.g., darknet markets, ransomware actors, DeFi platforms, mining pools, mixers, merchant services)
Advanced technical security certifications pertaining to cryptocurrency investigations or blockchain analysis (e.g., Chainalysis Investigation Specialist Certification [CISC], TRM Advanced Crypto Investigator [ACI], Elliptic Specialist Investigator Certification, Ciphertrace Cryptocurrency Tracing Certified Examiner [CTCE])
Formal foreign language training or competency, especially in Russian, Farsi, Chinese, Spanish, or Portuguese

About The Opportunity

Wavelo is looking to add a new member to our Analytics, Insights and Reporting team. Together, we’re responsible for all of the reporting, analytics, data flows, visualization, and related business intelligence operations within our quickly growing company, along with drawing insight from data and presenting this to various levels of the organization. We’ve got a lot of data, and we’re looking for someone to help us get the most out of it. To do that, you’ll need to be comfortable working end to end in the data pipeline; from extracting data from source systems into our data lake, to building visualizations and dashboards in Looker and everything in between.

What You'll Be Doing

Work with internal and external business, product, and engineering stakeholders to understand BI and analytics needs and priorities
Collaborate with data engineering team, other analysts, and stakeholders to understand data sources, develop data pipelines to transform raw data to clean & aggregated data, and develop BI solutions
Analyze KPIs to understand trends, glean insights, and present these findings to stakeholders at various levels
Work on business analytics projects incorporating predictive and prescriptive analytics to find valuable insights from data and help drive business decisions

Qualifications Required

Post-secondary education in Mathematics, Statistics, Computer Science, or another technical field
Excellent written & verbal communication skills, with the ability to gather requirements/communicate analysis from/to various internal & external clients
Top-notch interpersonal skills
Excellent math and statistical analysis skills, especially as they pertain to business and experimentation
Proficiency in the presentation and visualization of numbers and statistical data
Ability to understand business imperatives and drivers, find relevant data correlations, and create processes by which the data correlations are translated to information flows that help drive the business
5+ years of quantitative analysis work experience - experience in the Wireless/Telecom space would be considered a strong asset
5+ years experience handling, manipulating and analyzing data and creating analytical reports
Strong expertise with an SQL language (PostgreSQL would be an asset), as well with as database structures and data lake architectures
Strong knowledge of Microsoft Excel and Google Suite
Experience with Pentaho Data Integration would be an asset
Expertise in developing business intelligence solutions in Looker or other top BI software (e.g. Tableau, Power BI, etc.)
Proficiency with Python (preferred) or R
An understanding of the principles, tools, and processes of data science
Experience with Kafka would be an asset
